Responsibilities that the Government and the People Should Fulfill - Chairman Lin's New Year's Day Radio Address 81

Chairman Lin of the National Government delivered a speech at the Central Broadcasting Station at noon on New Year's Day, entitled "Responsibilities that the Government and the People Should Fulfill in the 25th Year of the Republic of China." The original text of his speech is recorded below. "Today is the New Year's Day of the 25th year of the Republic of China. I have a few words to offer to my fellow countrymen across the country. The Fifth National Congress resolved last year to convene the National Assembly within the 25th year of the Republic of China. Subsequently, the First Plenary Session resolved to announce the draft constitution on May 5, to complete the election of representatives to the National Assembly before October 10, and to convene the National Assembly on November 12. According to this resolution, we must unite as one and work together with the government this year in November in order to achieve twice the results with half the effort, to complete the mission entrusted to us by the Fifth National Congress, and to achieve the goal of completing autonomy and implementing constitutional government. Therefore, we feel that the responsibilities we bear this year are several times greater than last year. The more responsibility we can fulfill for the country, the more achievements the country will certainly be able to achieve. The more efforts our fellow countrymen across the country can make for the country, the more progress the country will certainly be able to make. If we can unite in good faith under this principle and work together, not only can local autonomy be completed on schedule, and constitutional government can be implemented on schedule, but also our country can turn from weakness to strength, we can raise our country's position in the international community, and we can promote the revival of our Chinese nation. The ancients said, 'The plan for the year lies in spring.' Today is New Year's Day, the beginning of spring, and it is also the day we start to refresh our spirits and intensify our work. From today onwards, everyone must fulfill their own responsibilities, and every hour must do an hour's worth of work. Everyone should contribute all their energy and all their intelligence to the country and to society, and we must earnestly follow the teachings of the President, taking loyalty, filial piety, benevolence, love, faith, righteousness, and peace as the foundation for cultivating ourselves and establishing virtue, and taking the Founding Strategy and the Founding Program as the compass for our country's nation-building and governance. The so-called cultivating oneself and establishing virtue requires everyone to be able to self-discipline and be honest in public service. If everyone can be self-disciplined and honest in public service, then the country's politics will naturally be clear, and the country's construction will naturally progress. The President's Founding Strategy and Founding Program that he showed us will naturally be fully realized. The President's will said, 'I have devoted myself to the national revolution for forty years, and its purpose is to seek freedom and equality for China.' If we now want to achieve the President's goal of seeking freedom for China, we must first contribute the freedom of individuals to the country, and gather the freedom of 400 million people to become the entire freedom of the Republic of China. If we want to achieve the President's goal of seeking equality for China, we must all fulfill more obligations and not compete for rights. Everyone should shoulder the obligations they should fulfill to the country, and everyone should contribute the private rights they should contribute to the country. Everyone should first seek equality of obligations, and not just seek equality of rights, and then the country will develop substantial strength and will achieve an equal position in the international community. We should all base ourselves on this meaning, everyone should set an example, sacrifice the freedom of each individual, and seek freedom for the country, and everyone should contribute their rights to the country and seek equality for the country. China's achievement of freedom and equality is not only the happiness of the Chinese people, but also the foundation of peace in East Asia will be further consolidated as a result, and it can maintain long-term peace in the world and promote the common happiness of mankind. Therefore, our current efforts as Chinese people are not only related to the survival of China itself, but will also affect the safety and security of the world. We should work hard for the sake of China's survival, and we should also work hard for the sake of the world's safety. This is my contribution to my fellow countrymen across the country today. I hope that all my fellow countrymen across the country will unite as one and work together from this day onwards. I am willing to encourage myself together with my beloved fellow countrymen across the country."

Capital Held Celebration of the Founding of the Republic of China 82

Central Party Headquarters Held Ceremony at Dr. Sun Yat-sen's Mausoleum, Chairman Lin Delivered a Speech on Behalf of the National Government

Central Party Headquarters: On the 1st at 9:00 AM, the Central Party Headquarters held a ceremony at Dr. Sun Yat-sen's Mausoleum to commemorate the founding of the Republic of China and to pay respects at the mausoleum. From Zhongshan Gate to the mausoleum's main avenue, military police and the Mausoleum Administration's security team had increased patrols in advance, maintaining strict security. Although snowflakes were falling and a cold wind was blowing, the attendees included Vice Chairman Chiang Kai-shek and Central Committee members Ye Chucang, Ju Zheng, Dai Chuanxian, Feng Yuxiang, He Yingqin, Zhu Peide, Ding Weifen, Zhang Ji, Jiang Zuobin, and over eighty others. There were approximately two hundred staff members above the rank of Secretary-General from the Central Party Headquarters, all faculty members and students (including recruits) from the Central Military Academy, and all faculty, staff, and students from the Central Political School, totaling several thousand people. The total number of participants was estimated to be over six thousand. Upon arriving at the mausoleum, everyone lined up according to the designated locations. Chairman Chiang Kai-shek, dressed in military uniform and wearing a sword, stood on the central stone steps in front of the memorial hall. All Central Committee members were dressed in blue robes and black mandarin jackets, arranged by age. Staff from the Central Party Headquarters wore blue cloth uniforms, and faculty and staff from the Central Political School wore military uniforms, standing on the right side of the platform. Thousands of students from the Military Academy and the Political School lined up along the stone steps, all the way to the stele in front of Dr. Sun Yat-sen's tomb at the bottom of the steps. At 9:00 AM sharp, music was played, and Vice Chairman Chiang Kai-shek led the ceremony, presenting wreaths from the Central Executive Committee and the Supervisory Committee. After the ceremony, Vice Chairman Chiang Kai-shek gave a speech, the gist of which was: "Comrades, soldiers, twenty-five years ago today, our Dr. Sun Yat-sen worked hard to revolutionize and overthrow the Qing Dynasty, liberate the Chinese nation, and bear the important task of establishing the Republic of China. It was on this day that he took office as the Provisional President of the Republic of China in the capital. What glorious and great history! And how honored and excited we are today to hold such a glorious and great commemoration in front of Dr. Sun Yat-sen's Mausoleum in the ice and snow. Everyone must know that today is the most glorious day for our Chinese nation and the most glorious day for our Kuomintang. I hope that all party members and compatriots across the country, during this extremely difficult period, will work hard to complete Dr. Sun Yat-sen's teachings to preserve this great glory. Finally, I wish all comrades and soldiers a happy and healthy New Year, and I wish everyone success in their aspirations." The speech lasted over thirty minutes, after which music was played to announce the end of the ceremony. As the meeting adjourned, Vice Chairman Chiang Kai-shek nodded to all Central Committee members, Central Party Headquarters staff, and senior Military Academy faculty to express his New Year's greetings.

National Government: The National Government held a celebration ceremony at 10:00 AM in the National Government Auditorium to commemorate the 25th anniversary of the founding of the Republic of China. Chairman Lin Sen, Chiang Kai-shek, and the presidents of the three Yuan (Executive, Legislative, and Judicial), as well as Ye Chucang, Chen Lifu, Deng Jiayan, Jing Hengyi, Zhou Zhenlin, Qin Zhen, and others, along with National Government staff, civil officials above the rank of Senior Rank and military officers above the rank of Colonel from various ministries and commissions, totaling over eight hundred people, attended. After Chairman Lin Sen led the ceremony, he delivered a speech, saying, "Everyone, today is the first day of the 25th year of the Republic of China, which is also the day twenty-five years ago when Dr. Sun Yat-sen took office as the Provisional President in Nanjing, the founding day of the Republic of China. As we recall how Dr. Sun Yat-sen founded the government amidst difficulties and hardships twenty-five years ago, and the various teachings he left us, we feel ashamed that there is still much work we have not yet fully accomplished. The ancients said to get rid of the old and establish the new. Although the old work has passed, it should still be reviewed. The new work should be diligently advanced. Our responsibility this year is even greater than last year because the Fifth National Congress decided last year that a National Assembly should be convened within the 25th year of the Republic of China. The First Plenary Session also decided that the draft constitution should be announced on May 5th this year, and the National Assembly should open on November 12th. Such major events cannot be accomplished without the whole country preparing wholeheartedly and making doubled efforts. Therefore, this year's work must be even more urgent than last year's. The draft constitution has already been discussed by the President of the Legislative Yuan and many experts across the country have also contributed their opinions. The Central Political Conference has also discussed it many times and a committee has been specially established to study the matter. However, there are still two key points in the draft, namely: 1. What obligations should citizens fulfill to the state and what rights should they enjoy? 2. How should the powers of the central government and local governments be defined to be appropriate? We still hope that all sectors of society across the country will contribute more opinions. The Central Government will definitely accept them sincerely during the study. Although May 5th is still several months away, the various preparations before the announcement of the draft constitution cannot be delayed. The procedures for convening the National Assembly are even more complicated because our country has a vast territory and a large population, and the situations in each province are not the same. To uniformly complete the election according to law requires the cooperation of the people and the government. This is my greatest hope today. We should ensure that these major events are completed on schedule so that constitutional government can be implemented as soon as possible, and the people can fully fulfill their obligations to the state and fully enjoy the rights granted by the state. Today is the first day of the 25th year. May everyone work together." After the speech, a group greeting ceremony was held. First, everyone bowed three times to Chairman Lin Sen, who returned the greeting. Then, civil and military officials bowed to each other once. Thus, the solemn celebration ceremony concluded amidst the melodious music.

Songjiang: Local Education Center Hosts Newspaper Exhibition 83

The first day of the 25th year of the Republic of China was the anniversary of the founding of the National Government. Various agencies held celebrations. Although it rained on that day, various agencies, schools, and organizations held group greeting ceremonies at their respective locations. The county government hosted a banquet on this day for leaders from all walks of life and heads of various agencies to mark the joyous gathering. The Local Education Center held a local newspaper exhibition from the first day of the new year to the third day, collecting various local newspapers from the city for public viewing. These included newspapers such as the "Political Review," "Rong Bao," (a newspaper from the founding year of the Republic) "Jiufeng Bao," and "Song Bao" (a newspaper from the fifth year of the Republic), all of which were hosted by well-known figures at the time. Their discussions were lively, and reflecting on those times provides valuable references for social changes.

Suzhou: Fire at Ye-Ci Teahouse 84

The Ye-Ci Teahouse on the main road outside Changmen, had been in operation for hundreds of years. According to legend, the owner of the store made his fortune from a Ye-Ci, hence the fame throughout Jiangsu and Zhejiang, and the business was booming. In recent years, due to the impact of the social downturn, liquidity became a problem, and Luo Jintang, the owner of Ling Jiahe Teahouse and Ziyangguan Wild Game Restaurant, took over the business. He had a goods fire insurance policy worth 2,800 yuan with the Lao Gongmao Company and a property decoration fire insurance policy worth 1,400 yuan with the Taiyang Company. On the second day, the store was empty and no one was inside. The employees had all left through the back door. As a result, in addition to the complete destruction of the store, the neighboring Yan Demao Tea Shop, Xin Xin Barber Shop, Jin Rui Xing Hotel, and other stores were also destroyed, totaling seven rooms. The building was owned by Yi Xing Real Estate Company, which also had a fire insurance policy worth 5,300 yuan with the Tianyi Company.

Wuxi: Hundreds of Refugees Loot Farmhouse 85

In Qianzhou Town, the ninth district under the county's jurisdiction, on New Year's Day, over two hundred refugees from Hunan arrived. The town head provided them with rations and escorted them out of the town by the business association. Unexpectedly, when the refugees arrived at Yinqiao in Tangping Township, the tenth district, they saw Zhou Yichun's family collecting dues. Without asking why, they broke into the house and looted 124.7 yuan and 180 yuan in silver, two gold buttons, several pieces of silk clothing, and other items before fleeing. Zhou Yichun, unwilling to accept the theft of his silver, went outside to report the incident. Neighbors rang gongs to gather people, intending to retrieve the stolen silver, and removed the bridge planks. Two refugees, Zhang Xiaofu and Zhang Xiaoqing, attempted to escape by swimming across the river but drowned. The refugees then made trouble for Zhou Yichun. The Qianzhou Business Association was informed and arrived at the scene to suppress the unrest. On the third day, Tu Zheng Zhou Deming reported the incident to the local court. Prosecutor Shen went to the countryside to investigate and confirmed that the two had died after falling into the river. Tu Zheng prepared coffins for burial, but the refugees refused and continued to cause disturbances in the village. The Yuqi Public Security Substation reported the situation to the Public Security Bureau and requested the dispatch of troops to the countryside to escort the refugees out of the area.

Nantong: Tongruhai Police and Troops Suppress Bandits 86

In the Erdao area of the Qi'an Town jurisdiction, over thirty bandits had infiltrated from the northeastern coast, robbing nearby towns and villages and killing police officers. Upon receiving the report, the District Security Command dispatched security teams from Nantong, Rugao, and Haimen counties on the third day to encircle and suppress the bandits, with city and rural police assisting in the blockade.

Furthermore, my late husband's concubine, Chen Jingqiu, has not returned to her hometown for several years. My division of property with my father and brother, Chu Yufeng, is well known to my relatives and cannot be swayed by rumors. I am writing to inform you of this, and I urge you to make a correction. Upon investigation, Police Officer Mao Jinzhang of this branch bureau requested a long leave of absence on November 27th and left the bureau. National Language Lecture: How to Write 88

Ye Shaojun, Editor of Kaiming Bookstore

Fellow students: Today's topic is "How to Write." There are many books on this topic, some called "Composition Methods" or "Essentials of Grammar," which explain it in great detail. When a person picks up a pen to write, it would be ridiculous to constantly refer to these books and do everything according to what they say, just like a housewife holding a cooking lecture and making dishes at the same time. Most of these books summarize rules from existing articles and tell people how to write in accordance with the rules, and of course, they also explain how to write against the rules. With this knowledge, we have a measuring tool to look at general articles, not only knowing that an article is good, but also being able to say where an article is good, not only knowing that an article is bad, but also being able to say where an article is bad. Naturally, this knowledge can also affect our writing habits, but this influence is only between intentional and unintentional. On a certain point, it was originally often against the rules, but because of the knowledge of grammar, we realize our illegality. So, we pay special attention to change him over. This special attention may not be effective immediately. Perhaps in three times, twice it has been changed, and once it still commits the old problem. It must become a habit from special attention without deliberation, so that it can be in accordance with the rules every time. Therefore, books on grammar mainly help us to enhance our eyesight in reading articles, and enhancing our writing wrist strength is only an indirect help. I am not advising you not to read these books, but just saying that reading these books may not be able to write articles well. If you go to these books when it comes to writing, it is even more stupid and useless.

You all write vernacular now. The highest realm of vernacular is that the article is the same as the speaking. The sentences written on the paper, when read, are the sentences of spoken language, teaching people to read and listen, not only to completely understand the meaning in the article, but also to be able to comprehend the tone and spirit, as if listening to the person who wrote the article speaking in person. To achieve this realm, you cannot specialize in writing, but the most important thing is to forge our language habits. Because language is like the object itself, and the article is like a photo that leaves an image of the object. The object itself is complete and has a pattern, and the photo taken is of course complete and has a pattern. The language is thorough and has no problems. The article written according to the language is often thorough and has no problems. Therefore, forging language habits is a way to find the source. However, one sentence should be stated, and language habits should be forged. A person lives in a crowd, and there is a need to speak at any time and anywhere. If there are various shortcomings in language habits, there are also shortcomings in living skills, which is very disadvantageous. Practicing good language habits, at least, has a very important life skill. At the same time, this is the most reliable source for writing. How can we not work hard to forge it?

There are speaking subjects in elementary schools, and there are also organizations such as speech debate meetings. In middle schools, speeches and debates are also often held. These are all ways to forge language habits. When participating in this kind of gathering, we listen quietly to the language of the person who speaks, often with the following situations. After saying half a sentence, he shrunk back and changed to another sentence, which has nothing to do with the half sentence just now. This is one kind. "However," "however" in a series, "then" "then" a big pile, as usual, using one is enough, only because it takes time to prolong the time, waiting for the following words, only said a lot, this is one kind. The place that should be "however" is not "however", and the place that should be "then" is not "then." It is only because there seems to be a word needed in this place, but there is no alternative, so I randomly pull a word to make up the number. This is one kind. Some words sound very harsh. After careful identification, it turns out that there are several words in it that are not very appropriate, or they have used too many or too few words. This is another kind. A person who speaks like this must have very poor language habits at ordinary times, and never pays attention to forging it, so he reveals his weaknesses in the speech and debate meetings. If he teaches him to write articles, he will naturally write according to his own language habits, then his article must be more difficult for people to understand than his spoken language. Because when he speaks, his facial expressions and body postures are used as help. Relying on these helps, although the language is a little bit worse, it can still make people understand the general idea. When it is written as an article, the facial expressions and body postures cannot be written in. What people see is only some broken sentences that do not match the beginning and the end. How can people not be confused? Because of my job, I have many opportunities to read articles by middle school students, some of which are very outstanding, and some of which are very ugly, which is the so-called incomprehensible. The two words incomprehensible are too general. To be more specific, the meaning contained in these two words, in addition to the unsound and inappropriate materials, is the several problems mentioned above, that is, the shortcomings of language habits. If these students usually pay attention to the forging language habits, they can reduce a part of the incomprehensible when writing articles. Add to this the tempering of experience to make the writing materials sound and appropriate, and then it is completely clear. The so-called "clear" is originally not a state that is out of reach:

How should we start forging language habits? This is not difficult, but you must have perseverance and treat it as one thing at any time and place, just like correcting the posture of sitting and standing. You must sit upright and stand upright at any time and place to develop the habit of sitting upright and standing upright. We must limit ourselves, no matter when, not to say an incomplete sentence, say a sentence, we must express a meaning, so that people can understand it when they listen to it. We must limit ourselves, no matter when, not to use a word that we do not understand very well in the language, nor to force a word that is not very appropriate in the language, and when we say a sentence, every word must be very competent, like a skilled officer commanding his soldiers. We must also limit ourselves, no matter when, not to use a conjunction indiscriminately, not to use more or less an auxiliary word, and when we say a sentence, we must "however" only in the place where we should "however", and "then" only in the place where we should "then", and do not lack "ma" where we need "ma", and do not unnecessarily "le" where we do not need "le." This kind of forging seems very superficial and ridiculous, but it is the most basic. Parents should supervise young children, and elementary school teachers should supervise elementary school students, teaching them to do this kind of forging. Unfortunately, parents and elementary school teachers have not paid attention to this level, or they have paid attention to it but have not received the corresponding effect. For the sake of completing extremely important life skills, we have to pay attention to it ourselves. After paying attention to it for a considerable period of time, we must measure the effect. From extremely short simple sentences such as "I am reading" and "He has eaten", we cannot see it in these languages. We might as well try to say five minutes of continuous words and see if every sentence in this speech can follow the conditions we set ourselves. If we can, then our forging has been effective. At this point, it is not difficult to write articles. What should be said orally should be written in writing. Writing down the invisible language into a tangible article, who wouldn't do it as long as Chu will write? And the incomprehensible in writing will not happen, because the original is the language that is completely free of problems.

Listening to other people's language and reading other people's articles is also helpful for exercising language habits. When listening to other people's language, if you don't pay special attention, then understanding other people's meaning is enough, and it will not directly help to forge our language habits. We must pay special attention to how people choose words, how people express a meaning, and how people say a long language in order. After this, the inspection is all useful information for us. We can imitate the strengths of others, and we can avoid the shortcomings of others. Let's talk about reading other people's articles. There is one point that must be noted here, that is, the current articles, even those written by famous article writers, are not purely spoken language. It has only been a dozen years since writing vernacular, and everyone's skills have not been trained to a very skilled level. At the same time, the vocabulary of vernacular has not been publicly selected. For the sake of convenience, everyone often mixes some classical tones and vocabularies to become a kind of awkward style. But we just said that the highest realm of vernacular is that the article is the same as the speaking. Therefore, this kind of awkward style can only be regarded as a natural product of the transitional period, and cannot be regarded as a fully perfect standard model? If this point is clearly understood, we can avoid the bad influence of the current articles and read with a critical eye. If there are advantages, we should of course imitate them, and try to avoid the short points that are not very pure. If middle school students all over the country work hard in this way, not only can their language habits be forged very well, but also the style of vernacular can be accelerated to the most pure realm? Our Country's Economic Sanctions Against Italy Have Been Implemented Since the Previous Day 91

The League of Nations previously sent a circular to all member states, unanimously implementing an economic blockade against Italy. Central Mint Officially Starts Minting Copper-Nickel Subsidiary Coins from the 6th 92

According to Shen Shi News Agency, after receiving orders to mint subsidiary coins, the Central Mint first had its Manufacturing Department Director cast several models, which were selected by the Ministry of Finance. Then, starting from December 20th of last year, they began trial minting of copper-nickel alloy subsidiary coins. These subsidiary coins are divided into six denominations: 50 cents, 20 cents, 10 cents, 5 cents, 2 cents, and 1 cent. Currently, the mint is trial minting the 1-cent subsidiary coin. The composition and color have been carefully adjusted by the mint's engineers. The minted subsidiary coins have been sent to the Ministry of Finance for review. It is now known that after several inspections, all have been found to be qualified. Therefore, the mint has decided to officially start minting the six denominations of subsidiary coins from the 6th of this month. In the future, after the Ministry of Finance announces it, these subsidiary coins can be circulated and used in the market, it is said. The mint has added seven days of night shifts from the 25th of last month, rushing to produce mint bars, and the work is extremely busy. The quantity is very large and has been sufficient. Starting from January of the 25th year, silver coins will be minted. According to the mint's announcement, since the Ministry of Finance promulgated the new legal currency system, the number of silver coins minted has reached more than 26 million yuan, all of which have been transported to the Central Bank to serve as reserves. In any case, it is sufficient to cope with scheduling and will not cause any panic. Therefore, there is currently no need to continue minting. However, types A and B of mint bars are frequently needed by various banks, so they are still being minted as usual, but the quantity is gradually reduced each month to meet the needs, it is said.

The United Federation of National Products Factories of Shanghai, for the difficulties felt by its member manufacturers, previously requested assistance from the government. Tianli Anhydrous Ammonia Products Factory Grand Opening on New Year's Day Afternoon 94

Minister of Industry Wu Dingchang Presided over the Opening Ceremony

The Tianli Anhydrous Ammonia Products Factory held its grand opening ceremony at 3 p.m. on New Year's Day. Minister of Industry Wu Dingchang came to Shanghai from Nanjing to participate and delivered a speech. Various agencies of the municipal government also sent representatives to attend. The factory uses the latest type of machinery and utilizes natural raw materials to manufacture important industrial raw materials such as nitric acid, which is a highlight in the history of our country's industry. The grand occasion of the opening ceremony is recorded as follows:

Venue Decoration The factory is located in Zhoujiadu, Shanghai West. Inside the factory building, the four walls are covered with silk banners sent by various parties, and the Party and national flags and emblems are hung. Fresh flowers are placed in front of the podium, and colorful paper is wrapped around as a cable, which is exceptionally beautiful. Wu Yun-chu and his staff personally greeted the guests who attended the meeting, including Wu Dingchang, Fan Xudong, Li Zhaohuan, Zou Bingwen, Xu Xinliu, Xu Peihuang, Pan Yangyao, Zhou Zuomin, Wu Yunzhai, Li Dachao, Qian Chengxu, Guo Chengen, Ji Zejin, Wang Ertao, Qian Xinzhi, Wen Yuqing, Chen Zheqing, and more than 500 Chinese and foreign guests.

Releasing Balloons When the guests signed in, each was given a ticket to receive a balloon. The name and address were written on the ticket and tied under the balloon. At the balloon releasing place, the balloons were released to add to the fun. For a time, colorful balloons flew around, which was dazzling. However, the torrential rain inevitably spoiled the fun. The three large silver balloons set up by the factory could not be raised due to low air pressure. If anyone finds the balloons released by the guests and sends the tickets to the factory, they can get a gift, it is said.

Ceremony Order At 3 o'clock sharp, the ceremony began, in the following order: 1. Music; 2. All stand at attention; 3. Pay the highest respect to the Party and national flags and the portrait of the Premier; 4. Chairman Zhu Ziqian reads the Premier's will; 5. Silent tribute; 6. Chairman Zhu Ziqian delivers the opening speech; 7. Wu Yun-chu reports on the preparation process; 8. Minister Wu and Director Qian deliver speeches; 9. Representative speeches; 10. Factory representative delivers a reply; 11. Minister Wu performs the opening ceremony; 12. Tour the factory, take photos, tea, and the ceremony is completed.

Preparation Process After the ceremony, Chairman Zhu Ziqian delivered the opening speech, saying: "Today is the opening of the Tianli Anhydrous Ammonia Factory. We are extremely grateful to the government officials and guests from all parties for braving the rain to participate. All the creation and planning of our factory are presided over by Mr. Wu Yun-chu. Please ask Mr. Wu to report on the preparation process in detail." Then Mr. Wu reported: "Four years ago, the government planned to jointly run a sulfuric acid factory with a British and German company. The Ministry of Industries appointed personnel to start preparations. However, at that time, the plan was too grand and the equipment was too large, so it was difficult to complete. Therefore, after several negotiations, there was no result. In the 21st year of the Republic, the American DuPont Company intended to sell the synthetic ammonia factory in Seattle. I happened to be traveling in Europe and America, so I went to inspect it and saw that its machinery was good, so I started negotiations. The agreement was reached in November, and then shares were raised to establish the company. It was established in January of the 23rd year of the Republic. Later, the Ministry of Industries ran its own sulfuric acid factory. In order to divide the work and cooperate, our factory focused on the manufacture of nitric acid. In July, I went to Europe again to inspect the machinery ordered and investigate the progress of nitric acid manufacturing methods. I returned to China in October and actively installed it. In August of the 24th year of the Republic, anhydrous ammonia was produced. In September, dilute nitric acid was produced. In October, concentrated nitric acid was produced. In November, the sulfuric acid concentration device was completed. The engineering part has come to an end. Today, I am honored to have you all here, and I hope to receive your guidance."

Ministerial Speech Minister of Industry Wu Dingchang gave a speech, saying: "It is very meaningful to participate in the opening ceremony of the Tianli Anhydrous Ammonia Factory on New Year's Day of the 25th year of the Republic. In the past ten years, our country has gradually developed in applied chemistry and chemical industry, which is a good phenomenon for the country. There is Mr. Fan Xudong in the north and Mr. Wu Yun-chu in the south among the domestic chemists. These two gentlemen are the leaders of our country's chemical industry, and almost everyone knows it. The gradual progress of our country's chemical industry should be given twelve points of respect to the two gentlemen. In the recent decades, the domestic economy has declined. Not only is it difficult to establish new factories, but also the old factories have failed one after another. The establishment of this new factory today is thought to be a sign of industrial turning point. Its development and prosperity are not only the glory of Mr. Wu's personal, but also the glory of the industrial community and the government and people. In the past, most of the factories built large houses first, which consumed most of the capital. The Tianli Factory seeks the perfection of machinery and equipment with almost all the capital. Its success can be expected, and its founding spirit can be a model for the Chinese people to run factories."

Guest Speeches Deputy Minister of Education Qian Changzhao said, "Anhydrous ammonia has a close relationship with the national economy and the people's livelihood. Our country's chemical industry is still in its infancy. The success of this Tianli Factory is something we can be happy about. The success of the Tianli Factory is the result of Mr. Wu's decades of hard work. Mr. Wu initially researched monosodium glutamate and obtained good results with a very small amount of capital. Its products are better than foreign products, but Mr. Wu is not satisfied with this. He also founded the Tianyuan Electrochemical Factory, and then established the Anhydrous Ammonia Factory today. His enterprising spirit is worthy of our admiration. This is one of the reasons. Starting with small-scale factories and then gradually seeking development. This is the second. In terms of technology, from simple to complex. This is the third. With these three characteristics, there are more successes and fewer failures. Moreover, in this recession, it was resolutely established, which can give the domestic industrialists unlimited courage. As for protection, encouragement and maintenance, the country and society should jointly bear the responsibility." Then Mayor Wu's representative Xu Peihuang, the representative of the National Federation of Industrial Unions Qian Chengxu, and others gave speeches. The speeches were omitted. Finally, Mr. Wu gave a thank-you speech, saying: "I am grateful to everyone for participating today, and I am also grateful to Minister Wu and others for their praise. I will work harder to meet your expectations. However, starting a business is not easy, and there are many difficulties. I hope that all sectors will guide me at any time." Then Minister Wu performed the opening ceremony. In the sound of long whistles, the ceremony was completed. The guests were led into the factory for a tour and then dispersed.

Bank Association Stops Announcing Exchange Rates from Yesterday; Domestic Exchange Rates Balanced After Legal Tender Implementation; Foreign Exchange Measures Implemented Yesterday; Exchange Rates Concentrated in the Central Bank, Bank of China, and Bank of Communications 95

The member banks of the Shanghai Banking Association, the banks of the Banking Reserve Committee, and the clearing houses, etc., opened for business yesterday. Measures to stabilize foreign exchange were implemented yesterday. Foreign exchange has been concentrated in the Central Bank, Bank of China, and Bank of Communications. The Market Committee of the Banking Association has stopped meeting and announcing exchange rates. The details are recorded as follows:

Stabilizing Foreign Exchange Measures Implemented After the Central Bank, Bank of China, and Bank of Communications conducted unlimited buying and selling of foreign exchange, and in order to stabilize foreign exchange, detailed measures were formulated. Foreign exchange purchased, before delivery, its funds existing in foreign banks can also be used as cash for issuance reserves. This has been implemented since yesterday. At the same time, the provisions of Article 4 of the Inspection Regulations of the Issuance Reserve Management Committee announced by the Ministry of Finance stipulate that "the cash reserve for legal tender issuance shall be 60%, which shall be filled with gold, silver or foreign exchange."

Fixed Exchange Rates for Foreign Exchange After the three banks made every effort to stabilize foreign exchange, the daily exchange rate for telegraphic transfer announced by the Central Bank is still in accordance with the standard amount. Yesterday's exchange rate was 1 shilling and 2.5 pence per yuan for London, 29.75 US dollars per 100 yuan for New York, 451 francs per 100 yuan for Paris, 73.75 marks per 100 yuan for Berlin, 103 yen per 100 yuan for Japan, and 94 Hong Kong dollars per 100 yuan for Hong Kong. In addition, the Foreign Exchange Parity Committee announced a balance tax rate of 1.325%.

Market Committee Stops Meeting In order to unify the business operations of the banks in the association, the Banking Association organized the Market Committee in accordance with the bill of October 8, 1920, with the purpose of unifying the market and jointly observing it. The members are Chen Zheqing, Zhang Peishen, Wang Yansong, etc. Each bank sends a representative to gather at the association at 9:00 am every day to discuss and decide on various domestic and foreign market prices. Now, since the banknotes of the Central Bank, Bank of China, and Bank of Communications are designated as legal tender, domestic exchange rates have been balanced, and foreign exchange is handled by the three banks. After the committee's resolution, it will stop announcing market prices by the association from this year, and the seventh article of the business rules, "The exchange rate of domestic and foreign exchange of domestic currency shall be determined and announced by the association every day," has been completely deleted. The market meeting at 9:00 am yesterday has been stopped.

Foreign Exchange Transactions Concentrated in Three Banks In addition to the Central Bank, Bank of China, and Bank of Communications, there are also Zhejiang Industrial, Shanghai Kenye, Siming, Continental, National Products, etc., among the Chinese-owned banks that operate foreign exchange. However, since the three banks are required to buy and sell foreign exchange without restriction, if there are foreign exchange transactions, they must be settled in accordance with the foreign exchange rate announced by the Central Bank, only earning commissions, so foreign exchange transactions have almost been concentrated in the three banks. At the same time, foreign banks such as Citibank, Mercantile Bank, HSBC, Banque de l'Indochine, Mitsui, Yokohama Specie Bank, Bank of Taiwan, Deutsch-Asiatische Bank, Nederlandsche Handel-Maatschappij, etc., are also limiting the purchase and sale of foreign exchange because there is no profit to be made. The member banks of the Banking Association, the banks of the Banking Reserve Committee, and the clearing houses, etc., opened for business yesterday. As for the amount of surplus of each bank, it will be announced after being collected by the Banking Association. In the future, all business will be suspended all day every Sunday. The new member banks of the Banking Association, Sichuan Meifeng, China Agricultural and Industrial, Zhejiang Local, Jiangsu Farmers, Yongda, and Pudong, etc., have all joined the clearing house. Yesterday's total exchange was 17,767,775.09 yuan.

Qian Industry is Ready for Complete Closure After the Qian Industry Association member qian shops and qian industry reserve banks and qian industry markets opened the day before yesterday, the decision was made to set January 23 as the final closure date for the 24th year, which is coming soon. All preparations have been made. For all customers, the settlement will be made on January 15, and statements will be issued. From January 19, the time for receiving tickets will be extended to 4:00 pm, and the return of tickets will be extended by one hour. Yesterday, the intraday interest rate in the Qian Industry Market was 9 points in both the morning and afternoon sessions.

Silk Exports Increased Sharply in the Past Eleven Months, But Imports of Rayon Also Increased 97

According to Shen Shi News Agency, silk exports in the past eleven months were worth more than 34,467,000 yuan, ranking second among all exports, only slightly less than tung oil by a hundred thousand yuan. The reason is that the American recovery movement has been effective, requiring a large amount of silk. The types of silk exported are as follows: Tonggong silk 491,893 yuan, white silk 512,178 yuan, white silk warp 1,273,428 yuan, white filature silk 22,023,428 yuan, grey filature silk 702,017 yuan, grey silk 4,610 yuan, yellow silk 368,888 yuan, yellow silk warp 33,976 yuan, yellow filature silk 1,867,871 yuan, waste silk 3,906,858 yuan, clothing 246,028 yuan, and silk waste cotton 7,739 yuan. The recovery of silk exports to second place is a good phenomenon in foreign trade last year. However, at the same time, imports of rayon have also increased sharply compared with before. In the past eleven months, rayon imports totaled 3,685,210 customs gold units, worth 6,660,898 yuan, an increase of more than 800,000 yuan compared with the import volume of 5,809,787 yuan in the same period of the previous year. The country with the most imports is Japan, worth 1,725,495 customs gold units. The second is Italy, worth 1,713,684 customs gold units, it is said.

Municipal National Products Year Sports Meet Urges the Use of National Products; Yesterday's Telegram to the Whole Country 98

The Municipal National Products Year Sports Meet, since its opening, specially telegraphed the whole country yesterday to unanimously use domestic products in order to promote the love of domestic products among the Chinese people. The original text says, (omitted above) The National Products Year has passed, followed by the Women's National Products Year. The Women's National Products Year has passed, followed by the Students' National Products Year. The Students' National Products Year has passed, and this year is officially designated as the Municipal National Products Year. The long continuation of this history of the National Products Movement makes us painfully realize that the effectiveness of the National Products Movement in recent years has only reached the external appearance of the national economy and has not yet penetrated into its inner layers. Therefore, if we want the full effect of the National Products Movement to be realized, we must rely on the continued efforts of our compatriots across the country. We pray that our compatriots across the country will pay close attention. In today's world, when hegemony is rampant and the world's economic panic has reached its peak, it is inevitable that imperialism will tightly seize the colonial market as the last colonial countries suffer even more cruel encounters. Since September 18, our country has lost its rights and territories, and the entire national economy has suffered from the poison of the dumping policies of the great powers and has fallen into an irrecoverable situation. This harsh fact clearly shows us that there is no other way to save the country except to promote domestic products and preserve the remaining economic lifeline. We further pray that our compatriots across the country will pay close attention. Imperialism's aggression against colonial countries must take two forms: one is the threat of force, and the other is economic exploitation. Attacking cities and seizing land or imposing various unequal treaties belongs to the former, and dumping goods and exploiting the blood of the colonial people belongs to the latter. Our country's current situation is undoubtedly trapped under the double attack of these two aggressions. Our compatriots across the country have all deeply regretted the humiliation and shame that our national army has failed to resist the unlimited aggression of the enemy troops in recent years. But we should also think that we have failed to isolate ourselves from foreign goods, and our daily lives are still surrounded by foreign goods, and we have not resisted them, which is also a humiliation and shame. Furthermore, our compatriots across the country all hate the treacherous merchants who are greedy for profit and forget their righteousness. But we should also think that we have failed to reject foreign goods and not use them, or we are accustomed to fashion and regard the use of imported goods as noble and beautiful, resulting in huge trade deficits and burying national interests. Asking ourselves, is it the same crime as the treacherous merchants? Compatriots, the national crisis is so serious that we can no longer be indecisive. We should quickly wake up, resolve to reject foreign goods, step onto the front line of the National Products Movement, and be a warrior in the national economic struggle. Promoting domestic products is the only way to save the country and survive, as mentioned above. Now, what we want to examine more is why the National Products Movement has failed in the past, and how should we promote it in the future to avoid repeating the same mistakes? Indeed, the exploitative desire of imperialism is difficult to fill, and the blood of the Chinese people has only the last drop left. Therefore, we must make the greatest efforts to open up the future for this newly born Municipal National Products Year. Examining the goals of the National Products Movement, we must not only ensure that everyone uses domestic products, but also that everyone has good domestic products to use and cheap domestic products to use. Therefore, we have determined the three principles of the National Products Movement to be the guidelines for our work: First, promote the psychological construction of the National Products Movement. This is to use the power of propaganda to stimulate the patriotic psychology of the 400 million compatriots and arouse the enthusiasm of everyone to use domestic products. For this, we will adopt various methods such as publishing, lecturing, and broadcasting to expand the promotion and introduction of domestic products. Second, promote the social construction of the National Products Movement. This is to change the social fashion of worshiping foreign goods and eliminate the traces of unscrupulous merchants. For this, we will hold various national product exhibitions and pavilions so that the public has the opportunity to recognize, purchase, and criticize national products, and strictly implement investigations and inspections to report and study them. Third, promote the material construction of the National Products Movement. This is to ensure that there are good domestic products and cheap domestic products to meet the needs of compatriots across the country. For this, we will ask the government to encourage livelihoods and remove all chains that bind domestic products, seek the development of transportation to facilitate the collection of raw materials and the transportation of manufactured goods, and contact various national product factories to improve manufacturing and reduce profits to alleviate the burden on users. This psychological, social, and material construction of the National Products Movement is the cornerstone of the national economy and the foundation of national rejuvenation. However, due to the arduous and complex nature of the work, in addition to our urban citizens who should focus on the central mobilization in name and in fact, we also hope that compatriots across the country will work together with one heart, rise up together, and with a calm and persevering spirit, bravely advance toward the path of "national products save the country."

Mayor Wu's Health Slightly Uncomfortable 99

Mayor Wu has felt slightly unwell since the day before yesterday. Yesterday, he went to the Municipal Government to review important official documents for only one hour, and then returned to his residence to rest and declined to meet with guests, it is said.

Various Groups Telegraph Government Regarding the Wu Case, Urging the Arrest of the Culprits 100

The late Mr. Wu Tingsheng, former chairman of the Shanghai Chinese Tobacco Industry Association, had been involved in the tobacco business for forty years, holding a leading position in the industry. In 1932, recognizing the increasing volume of imported tobacco leaves and the significant revenue leakage, he gathered Chinese capital to establish the Xuchang Tobacco Leaf Co., Ltd., aiming for cooperation in production, sales, and transportation. In 1934, he proposed a plan to improve American tobacco varieties to the Ministry of Finance. Minister Kong deeply praised his efforts, and in July of that year, a declaration was issued, allocating 50,000 yuan from funds for assisting in anti-smuggling and improving tobacco leaves to establish the American Tobacco Leaf Improvement Committee under the Taxation Administration of the Ministry of Finance. Mr. Wu was appointed as a full-time member to take charge of the project. For improving tobacco leaves, Mr. Wu established cultivation fields and distributed American tobacco seeds and temperature charts to farmers, meticulously planning various improvement measures, which have yielded positive results. Regarding the purchase and sale of tobacco leaves, he not only strived for cooperation in production, sales, and transportation but also paid attention to the supply and demand of tobacco leaves and the prevention of illicit tobacco. In addition, he devised and implemented practical measures to promote benefits and eliminate malpractices, such as cracking down on weight overages, mixed bundles, and mixed packaging, and standardizing silver exchange rates, and reported them to the Ministry of Finance for record-keeping to ensure the tobacco leaf trade was conducted fairly. Both merchants and farmers benefited, and local farmers deeply respected him. However, Mr. Wu's impartial handling of matters, regardless of hardship and complaints, greatly inconvenienced those who sought personal gain, and they harbored resentment, plotting to harm him. On the afternoon of December 30th of the previous year, at 3:00 PM, they instigated thugs to ambush him at the gate of Xuchang, and Mr. Wu was unfortunately assassinated. Those who heard the news from afar were deeply saddened. When the tragic news reached Shanghai, Mr. Wu's fellow villagers, relatives, and friends were extremely indignant. The Ministry of Finance, the Taxation Administration, the Ningbo and Fenghua Shanghai Fellow Villagers' Associations, the American Tobacco Leaf Improvement Committee of the Taxation Administration of the Ministry of Finance, the Anti-Smuggling Assistance Committee, the Tobacco Business Committee, and Mr. Wu's family have separately telegraphed President Chiang of the Executive Yuan and Minister Kong of the Ministry of Finance, requesting a thorough investigation and arrest of the mastermind and accomplices to uphold the law and console the deceased. Excerpts of the telegrams are recorded below:

Telegram from the Taxation Administration Urgent, Addressed to Minister Kong of the Ministry of Finance, Nanjing: According to a telegram from the Tobacco Business Committee, the family of Chairman Wu Tingsheng reported that he was assassinated in Xuchang West Street while on duty, which is extremely tragic. Please forward this request for the arrest of the culprits to console the deceased. Chairman Wu has been enthusiastic about committee affairs and spared no effort. He has been particularly diligent in assisting anti-smuggling and improving tobacco leaves, breaking through personal connections and handling matters impartially. However, villains have harbored resentment and taken the opportunity to attack, which is extremely unlawful. Please promptly forward this to the Ministry of Finance and telegraph the Henan Provincial Government to order the arrest of the culprits and bring them to justice. Furthermore, the Anti-Smuggling Assistance Committee, the American Tobacco Leaf Improvement Committee, and Mr. Wu's family have sent telegrams with similar requests. Adviser Wu Tingsheng has assisted in anti-smuggling and improved tobacco leaves for years, not avoiding hardship and complaints, and has devoted himself to the work, increasing public revenue and improving the tobacco business with considerable success. However, he was suddenly attacked and killed, which is truly regrettable. In light of the above, it is proposed that you promptly telegraph the Henan Provincial Government to order the arrest of the culprits within a time limit and bring them to justice to uphold the law and order. Respectfully submitted, Wu Qiding, Director of the Taxation Administration, sealed.

Telegram from the Ningbo Fellow Villagers' Association Addressed to President Chiang Kai-shek of the Executive Yuan, Nanjing: We were shocked and outraged to hear the news report that Mr. Wu Tingsheng was assassinated in Xuchang. We request that you telegraph the Henan Provincial Government to order the arrest of the culprits within a time limit and bring them to justice to console the deceased and punish the lawbreakers. Respectfully submitted, Yu Hede and others of the Shanghai Fellow Villagers' Association of Ningbo.

Telegram from the Fenghua Fellow Villagers' Association Addressed to Chairman Chiang Kai-shek of the Capital, our esteemed fellow villager: Your Excellency has made great contributions to the Party and the nation, striving for production and construction, which is admired by all. Mr. Wu Tingsheng, a fellow villager, has always supported the Party and the nation, serving the public interest. For the development of national tobacco, he has been diligent and enterprising. In recent years, he has upheld your intentions and carried out the orders of the Ministry of Finance, first improving tobacco varieties and regulating the market in Xuchang, benefiting hundreds of thousands of farmers, increasing production by more than ten million yuan annually, significantly increasing tax revenue, and reducing foreign tobacco imports. However, those who sought personal gain disregarded national production and the livelihood of farmers, initially designing obstructions, then confusing right and wrong, and even instigating thugs to inflict death. They have disregarded the law and order to the extreme, and national power has been weakened, and production has been damaged, which is unforgivable. We earnestly request that you protect the progress of production and construction and exercise the justice of eliminating violence and ensuring peace, promptly ordering the arrest of the culprits and investigating the masterminds so that Mr. Wu Tingsheng's principles may be made clear, and his grievances may be redressed. The entire Shanghai Fellow Villagers' Association is deeply grateful and awaits your instructions urgently. Respectfully submitted, Fenghua Fellow Villagers' Association.

Recently, he upheld the state's policy of promoting production and construction, carrying out the Ministry of Finance's order to improve tobacco varieties in Xuchang, Henan, in the original tobacco-producing area. Since the improvement, there has been success, not only has foreign imports sharply decreased, but also production has greatly increased, and tax revenue has gradually become abundant, and the beneficiaries are no less than tens of millions of farmers. Unexpectedly, a few villains, harboring evil intentions, intentionally sabotaged, causing Mr. Wu to be tragically assassinated before completing his meritorious work. Thinking of this, we are deeply saddened. We believe that eliminating violence and ensuring peace is a constant principle of the state, and we hope that loyal and virtuous people can be rewarded and encouraged, and that traitors and villains cannot escape punishment. Our association cherishes his past contributions and mourns the loss of a capable person for the state and society. Therefore, we especially request that you promptly order the local officials to strictly arrest the ringleaders and clearly execute them to console the loyal soul and uphold the law. We await your instructions with the utmost urgency.

The Jiangxin Steamer and the Yunlong Steamer Collided in the Middle of the River Yesterday; The Jiangxin Was More Severely Damaged but Can Still Manage to Sail to Shanghai 103

The Jiangxin, a first-class steamer of the state-owned China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, has a deadweight of 3,375 tons, a registered tonnage of 2,101 tons, a length of 340 feet, a width of 47 feet, a draft of 12 feet 6 inches, a horsepower of 2,200, and three decks. It left Hankou fully loaded with cargo and passengers on the night of the 3rd of this month to return to Shanghai. Unexpectedly, yesterday morning (the 4th), it was hit and damaged while traveling through Huangshi Port.

Collision En Route In recent days, the water level in the upper reaches of the Yangtze River has been decreasing daily, and there has been fog on the river surface. The Jiangxin was proceeding in Huangshi Port when the Yunlong steamer of the Heng'an Shipping Company, with a deadweight of 1,777 tons, was traveling from the lower reaches of the Yangtze River to Hankou. When it reached Huangshi Port and met the Jiangxin, the pilot was careless due to the shallow water and fog, resulting in a collision with the Jiangxin. Mr. Xu Bin, the captain of the Jiangxin, tried to retreat urgently, but it was too late, resulting in the collision and the accident.

Damage Situation After the accident, the captain of the Jiangxin immediately sent an urgent telegram to Shanghai to report to the head office. The telegram was very brief, stating that the ship was collided with by the Yunlong in the waters of Huangshi Port, and the hull on the starboard side, the railings and guardrails on the deck, and the cabins were damaged. Fortunately, it was above the waterline and did not affect navigation, and it could still sail to Shanghai. The Yunlong was also slightly damaged. The cause of the accident and the detailed situation are still awaiting further reports. Yesterday afternoon, the bureau received the telegram and found that the information was not detailed enough to understand the truth. In addition to sending a telegram to the captain of the ship for further inquiry, it first sent the received telegram to the insurance company for review. On the one hand, because the Jiangxin could arrive in Shanghai tomorrow, and today is Sunday, it was decided to wait until the ship arrives in Shanghai before inquiring the captain and sending technicians on board to inspect the ship, and then repair the damaged parts in the dock.

Ship Grounding Report, Hope to Be Saved Soon 104

Hengshan The Hengshan, a Yangtze River steamer of the Sanbei Company, has a deadweight of 1,922 tons and a length of 262 feet. The company received a telegram from its captain, Tao Jiexun Targersen, yesterday, stating that the ship ran aground downstream of Jiujiang at 4:00 PM on the 2nd of this month due to the sharp decline in river water. The ship was fully loaded with cargo and had a draft of 16 feet, so it could not move after running aground. The captain telegraphed Shanghai for help. The Qingpu steamer, which departed from Shanghai to Hankou at the end of last month, passed through Jiujiang on the 3rd, and the company telegraphed it to rescue the Hengshan. The Qingpu towed from 10:00 AM to 3:00 PM on the 3rd, but failed to rescue the Hengshan because it was stuck in the sand. The company was deeply concerned that the water level would continue to decline, making it difficult to rescue the ship. Yesterday afternoon, it urgently telegraphed the Jiujiang branch to send barges to unload the cargo from the ship before towing it.

Baofeng The Baofeng, a ship of the Jufeng Baoji Shipping Company, ran aground on the 1st of this month south of Songjigang after departing from Shanghai at 2:05 AM due to fog. The captain, Xue Jinlong, immediately tried to reverse the engine to escape, but the right propeller of the engine was damaged. It managed to retreat from the shoal at 3:10 AM. Yesterday, the Baofeng barely sailed back to Shanghai and reported to the company and the insurance company, preparing for repairs and the installation of a new propeller.

Oil Tanker A Sanbei Company oil barge ran aground above Yuezhou due to the falling water level. The barge is now surrounded by water and is almost on the beach. The Changsha branch sent a ship to rescue it, but it could not get close. The Shanghai bureau telegraphed the Hunan branch to send a large number of workers to dig and divert the river water to the bottom of the ship, hoping to tow it out of the shoal.

Wusong The Wusong, a Yangtze River ship of the British Taikoo Company, departed from Shanghai on the night of the 2nd of this month, fully loaded with cargo and passengers, heading for Hankou. Yesterday, Shanghai received a telegram stating that the ship ran aground near Jiangyin due to the falling river water and excessive load and could not move. The company has received the report and is planning towing and rescue procedures.

The Ministry of Finance Approved that Stamps Should Be Affixed to Supplementary Goods Lists 107

After the Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce submitted a request to the Ministry of Finance to exempt supplementary goods lists from stamp duty, the Ministry of Finance issued a reply yesterday with document number Shui Zi 8249, which stated, "I have received your telegram. After investigation, supplementary goods lists are given to the other party for the purpose of paying for the goods, which is a document for the payment of goods and not merely an inquiry. Therefore, when handing them over to the other party, stamps should be affixed according to the fifth item of the stamp duty rate table, the example of documents for the payment of goods. Please inform them of this."

Record of the Opening of the Party and National Flag Manufacturing and Sales Headquarters on New Year's Day 108

The Party and National Flag Manufacturing and Sales Headquarters, located in Jiyi Lane, Tianjin Road in this city, was approved by the Propaganda Department of the Central Party Headquarters and the Ministry of Interior and was established on November 20th of last year. It officially opened on New Year's Day this year (the opening ceremony was held at 3:00 PM that afternoon in the headquarters' auditorium, presided over by Zhang Zilian, chairman of the headquarters' management committee. Pan Gongzhan, a member of the Central Committee specially dispatched by the Central Propaganda Department and the Director of Education of this city, Lu Xirong, the Director of Rites and Customs of the Ministry of Interior, Lin Yannan dispatched by the Shanghai Municipal Government, and Lu Jingshi dispatched by the Municipal Party Headquarters, attended the bureau to deliver speeches on behalf of the government. Attendees included Chen Qicai, the Director of the Budget Office, Liu Derong, a special commissioner stationed at the bureau by the Central Propaganda Department, Li An, a special commissioner stationed at the bureau by the Ministry of Interior, and leaders from all walks of life such as Du Yuesheng, Shen Tianxin, Zhao Xichen, and Shen Zhongyi, totaling more than 300 people. Changrong Chu and Chi Tingxian, standing committee members of the bureau, and committee members Yu Zhendong, Deng Zhonghe, Weng Shou Xuan, Chen Zhibei, and Shen Chuchen were responsible for the reception. The details are recorded below.

Chairman's Speech Chairman Zhang Zilian delivered the opening speech, saying, "Today is the opening day of our headquarters. We are deeply honored to have representatives from the Central Party Headquarters, the Ministry of Interior, the Shanghai Municipal Government, and the Municipal Party Headquarters to deliver speeches, as well as distinguished figures from all walks of life to attend and provide guidance. The Party and National Flag is a symbol of the nation and the country, created by revolutionary martyrs who shed their blood to build the nation. Its colors and patterns symbolize the Three Principles of the People and the national spirit of peace and struggle. Before the establishment of this headquarters, which was approved by the Central Propaganda Department and the Ministry of Interior, the unified Party and National Flag movement was initiated by my request and approved and commended by Chairman Chiang. After the painstaking planning of the Party and government agencies, this headquarters was established. From now on, the colleagues of this headquarters should strive to fulfill the duties of a national citizen, promote and publicize the Party and National Flag, promote the national spirit, and devote ourselves to the national revival movement to live up to the expectations of the Central Party Headquarters, the Ministry of Interior, and compatriots from all walks of life."

Representative's Speech Pan Gongzhan, the representative of the Propaganda Department of the Central Party Headquarters, delivered a speech, saying, "The definition of a country has certain regulations in political science and law, but the symbol that represents the life and all the purposes of the country is the national flag. Our country builds the nation with the Party. Dr. Sun Yat-sen led the revolution with the Three Principles of the People. Since the Xingzhonghui and Tongmenghui to the Kuomintang, the history of the Republic of China has been deeply related to the Party. Now that the constitutional government has not yet been implemented, the Kuomintang is the highest leader in all aspects of national politics, so the Blue Sky with a White Sun Party flag should be respected together with the national flag. In the past, the size of the Party and National Flag did not meet the proportions, and the colors did not follow the prescribed standards, which was not conducive to showing neatness and magnificence. Therefore, there must be a unified method. The Party and National Flag Manufacturing and Sales Headquarters, under the leadership of Party and government agencies, is different from ordinary businesses and should assist the government in promoting the Party and National Flag. At this time of national crisis, we should pay attention to the promotion of the Party and National Flag to test the people's faith in the Party and the country. If all the compatriots in the country have the heart to support the Party and the country, the revival of the Chinese nation will not be difficult." Lu Xirong, the representative of the Ministry of Interior and the Director of Rites and Customs, delivered a speech, saying, "The Party and National Flag is a symbol and spiritual representation of the entire nation and country, which is of great importance in international perception. At this time when the entire nation is striving to revive the national movement, we should pay special attention to the Party and National Flag, which symbolizes the entire nation and country, and strive for neatness and uniformity. The Ministry of Interior has repeatedly issued regulations on the manufacturing and use of the Party and National Flag and the management of Party and National Flag manufacturing and sales stores in accordance with the instructions of the central government. However, flag merchants in various places are mostly small-capital operations, making it difficult to achieve uniformity. The Party and National Flag Manufacturing and Sales Headquarters was established after the Shanghai Textile Printing and Dyeing Company and the China Flag Manufacturing Company were approved to merge. The equipment and scale are sufficient to undertake the task of unifying the flag system and selling it throughout the country. Under the guidance and supervision of the Central Propaganda Department and the Ministry of Interior, it will be able to improve and achieve perfection." Lu Jingshi, the representative of the Municipal Party Headquarters, then delivered a speech with many words of encouragement. Chen Gongcai, the Director of the Budget Office, and Du Yuesheng and other leaders from all walks of life in this city also delivered speeches. Liu Derong, a special commissioner of the Central Propaganda Department, stated the importance that the Central Party Headquarters attached to the Party and National Flag, the methods and approvals prescribed by previous meetings, and the establishment of the Party and National Flag Manufacturing and Sales Headquarters by the Shanghai Textile Printing and Dyeing Company and the China Flag Manufacturing Company. Chairman Zhang Zilian then delivered a speech of thanks.

Reception for All Walks of Life After the ceremony, the headquarters hosted a banquet at the Jinlong Hotel to entertain the representatives of the Central Propaganda Department and the Ministry of Interior, as well as all walks of life in this city. All the committee members attended the reception, which was very grand for a while.

French Consulate General Hosts Reception for French Nationals on New Year's Day 110

The French Consulate General in Shanghai held a reception on Wednesday (New Year's Day) to celebrate the New Year. Many of the major French nationals and French army and navy officers in this city attended. Therefore, at around 11:00 AM, the east end of the Avenue Joffre was filled with parked cars, and several police officers were on the scene to take care of them. The guests were received by the French Consul General Bargeton and the staff of the consulate in accordance with the etiquette. After exchanging greetings, Mr. Bargeton gave a speech detailing the achievements of the French Concession in 1935 and said that there were 251 armed robbery cases in the Concession in 1934, which was reduced to 217 cases in 1935, with 137 cases solved and 217 people arrested. The total number of arrests in 1934 was 151. There were two armed kidnapping cases in 1935. The police had nine gun battles with bandits, resulting in the death of two police officers, the injury of one auxiliary police officer, one escape, and three other police officers injured. Four bandits were killed and two were injured. Also, in 1935, the number of strikes in the Concession was greatly reduced compared to the previous year. Mr. Bargeton also expressed his regret for the death of Tang Youren in the Concession. He then told the guests that they were living in a foreign country and that for the benefit of French businesses, all French nationals should unite. Without this, they could not obtain the cooperation of the Chinese people around them. He then praised the late French Ambassador to China, Wilden, and his successor, Nagy, for their contributions to the French nationals in China. He then raised a toast, played the Marseillaise, and everyone dispersed in joy.

Record of the Trial of the American Eastern Bank Case: This case involves a wide range and will require a long time to reach a final verdict. 113

Former general manager of American Eastern Bank (currently in liquidation), Mr. Raye, and vice president, Mr. Blanc, were recently indicted by the American District Attorney, Mr. Watson, and special assistant Dr. Slater, representing the U.S. government, in the U.S. Court for China on sixteen counts of embezzlement, fraud, and corruption. On Wednesday afternoon, Chief Judge Mr. Helmick opened the trial. This case is the most sensational one handled by the U.S. Court for China since the 1927 case in which District Attorney Mr. Hussa was accused of accepting bribes. Therefore, the audience was packed yesterday. The defendant, Mr. Raye, was represented by Tianjin lawyer Mr. Evans, while Mr. Blanc was represented by lawyers Mr. Fackling and Mr. Watson. After the court opened, Dr. Slater stated the main points of the charges against the defendants. Subsequently, Mr. Evans refuted them in a few words and formally declared the defendant not guilty. This case involves a wide range. According to Dr. Slater, the witnesses to be summoned in the future will be divided into five major categories for separate trials. Afterwards, Chief Judge Mr. Helmick announced the adjournment and scheduled the trial to continue at 10:00 AM next Monday. Judging from the case presented by Dr. Slater the other day, this case will definitely take a long time to reach a final verdict.

General Mobilization for River Dredging in the County: A total of twelve rivers to be dredged, starting work uniformly today. 114

Shanghai County has been levying labor for river dredging annually. The river channels to be dredged in the 24th year were previously reported separately by each district to the county government for review and approval. A dredging plan was also drafted by Chief Technical Officer Qi and submitted to the provincial department for approval. The rivers to be dredged include Hengli, Wanghaitang, Donghejing, Wushujing, Xuanzijing, Shenjingbang, Xinjinggang, Tangjiabang, Xiaohuangpu, Dongjingpinggang, and Xichangbang, a total of twelve rivers. Now, the county government believes that this agricultural off-season should be immediately implemented for dredging. Therefore, it is scheduled to start work uniformly on the 5th of this month (today), and it is expected that all will be completed around May.

Number of Flood Victims in Shandong Province Reaches Over 2 Million 116

The Shanghai Association for Raising Funds for Flood Relief in Various Provinces received a letter from the Shandong Yellow River Flood Relief Committee, stating that on July 10th this year, the Dongzhuang Linpu Collection in the upper reaches of the Yellow River in Shandong Province breached, flooding more than ten counties including Juancheng. Fields, houses, and grains were all swept away, and the mainland became a watery country, turning farmers into flood victims. The severity of the disaster is unprecedented in decades. Fortunately, the Shandong provincial government has been providing emergency relief while ordering various cities and counties to set up shelters. A total of 88 cities and counties have set up shelters, accommodating a total of 345,475 people, including the elderly and weak in the disaster area. In addition, in the ten disaster-stricken counties, at least 1.8 million people are without clothing or food and are registered for relief. The committee has already reported the situation by telegram in October. Currently, the floodwaters in the disaster area have not yet receded, and there is no hope for planting wheat, and there is no guarantee for spring plowing. In the long run, the flood victims in the shelters are provided with food, but their return date is uncertain. Those registered for relief are crying out all day long and have no means of livelihood. Moreover, it is deep winter, and clothing for warmth is especially needed. The tragic situation of the disaster has reached its extreme. The committee is responsible for relief and is undeniably obligated, but the relief funds depend entirely on the government and various charitable organizations and benevolent people for continuous support, working together to provide assistance. Now, the list of 345,475 flood victims sheltered in various cities and counties, and the 1,996,958 flood victims registered for relief in the ten disaster-stricken counties has been compiled. You are requested to check and assist the association, and please forward it to various charitable organizations. Thank you. Furthermore, the five counties of Zou, Teng, Wen, Shouzhang, and Yanggu have also been affected by the Yellow River breach, and the disaster situation is severe. Funds have been allocated for separate relief efforts. As for the number of flood victims, the order to investigate has not yet been returned, and it will be announced later. This is attached for your information. The disaster situation in various provinces this year, such as that in Shandong Province, covers as many as nine provinces, and the urgency of relief has increased rather than decreased. It is hoped that the entire country will rise up to provide emergency relief in order to achieve results.

Huafeng Flour Mill: Two Thieves Stealing Leather Belts Apprehended: Wang Caixi and Ma Yao 118

At 11:30 last night, five or six thieves suddenly came to the Huafeng Flour Mill on Xiaoshadu Road in West Shanghai. They went to the machine room and stole dozens of leather belts from the machines.
