Xinzha Branch: Cracking Down on Counterfeit Currency Manufacturing Organization: Ten Male and Female Criminals Arrested: Over 20,000 in Counterfeit Currency Seized: Two Machines and Many Parts 122

At approximately 10:00 AM on the 31st of last month, the Zhongyu Road Police Station of the Zhabei Xinzha Branch cracked down on a counterfeit currency manufacturing organization in the stove room at No. 38 Yuqing Lane, Xinyu Road, Qiujiang Road, and arrested a total of ten male and female suspects, including printing workers and apprentices. 12,000 yuan of single-sided counterfeit banknotes of the Chinese Farmers Bank that had been printed, 10,000 yuan of counterfeit banknotes in the initial version, and two machines were seized. The details are recorded as follows:

Superficial Details of the Organization: The location is at No. 38 Yuqing Lane (i.e., the first lane on the left south of Xinyu Road) on Qiujiang Road. It is a single-opening Japanese-style house, facing south from the north. Usually, people enter and exit from Xinyu Road in Yuqing Lane. The back door is directly connected to the municipal house on Qiujiang Road, with only a small lane in between. No one enters or exits, so it is locked all year round. In front of this house, in the living room, there is an Jiangxingji Machinery Factory, with many rusty old machines and rusty iron all over the ground. Therefore, the neighbors on the left and right do not go to see it, so no one knows that there is a counterfeit currency manufacturing organization.

Accidental Crackdown: Last month, the 31st was the last day for forced registration of opium smokers, so Inspector Xie Zhongyi of the Zhongxing Road Police Station sent patrol officers on the day shift to investigate household by household in the area under the jurisdiction of the police station to see if there were any opium smokers who had not registered. When police officer Wang Yingwen investigated the machinery factory, he saw that the door of the stove room was tightly closed. He ordered the second landlord, Jiang Yushan, to open the door, but Jiang replied that there was no one in the room, but the door was not locked. Police Officer Wang became even more suspicious. At first, he thought there must be opium smokers in the room. Who knew that after opening the door, he saw two printing machines? When asked what they were printing, the workers and apprentices replied that they were cigarette cards. Police Officer Wang ordered them to take them out to see. At first, the worker only took out a single sheet of watermarked double-sided counterfeit banknotes. The police officer could not see it clearly, so he took it himself from the shelf to read. He then saw that it was a single-sided counterfeit banknote of the Chinese Farmers Bank with a double bill of one yuan that had already been printed. He then realized that it was a counterfeit currency manufacturing factory. At this time, Jiang already knew that it could not be concealed and repeatedly begged for mercy, so he promised to bribe him with 100 yuan in national currency. The police officer falsely claimed that the matter was of great importance and that the amount of 100 yuan was too small, and then left for further discussion. Jiang thought that the accident could be avoided. Who knew that after the police officer left the door, he ran to the nearby guard post police officer Zhang Runxi and came back together. Police Officer Zhang guarded the workers and others, and Police Officer Wang ran out to call the Zhongxing Road Police Station. After receiving the report, Inspector Xie Zhongyi immediately led police chiefs Li Qingyun, Hao Likai, and Zhuang Jingzao to arrive and arrested all the people.

Names of the Criminals Arrested: Second landlord Jiang Yushan, 35 years old, from Anhui; printing workers Gu Linggen, 26 years old, from Changshu; Tian Mingyuan, 32 years old, from Changzhou; Zhang Linsheng, 34 years old, from Changshu; apprentices Jiang Yuanhe, 26 years old, from Anhui; Yang Ermao, 17 years old, from Shanghai; Jiang Yanggou, 16 years old, from Anhui; Zhang Hualang, 20 years old, from Shaoxing; Shen Amao, 16 years old, from Ningbo; suspect Zhao Xu, 42 years old, from Changshu; a total of ten people were arrested.

Evidence Seized: 12,000 yuan of red single-sided printed double bills of the counterfeit Chinese Farmers Bank banknotes were seized on the spot, along with 10,000 yellow initial versions of watermarked double bills of counterfeit banknotes, two lead seals, two machines, a total of 36 items, two models of counterfeit Chinese Farmers Bank banknotes, 25 lead blocks, a front mercury plate, a reverse mercury plate, three boxes of colored oil, etc. After being taken back to the station, they confessed that the main culprit in this case (i.e., the boss) was Wang Ziliang, the husband of Zhao Xu, who had gone out to buy things and were all on the run. After a brief interrogation by Inspector Xie, they were immediately escorted to the Xinzha Branch and transferred to the Public Security Bureau for interrogation.

Completion of the Tomb of the Unknown Heroes: Date of Completion Ceremony Set: Total Construction Cost Over 100,000 Yuan: Magnificent and Imposing, Worthy of Adoration by Future Generations 123

In order to commemorate the soldiers and civilians who died in the "January 28th" Shanghai War, the Gu Gongtuan of this city and leaders from all walks of life raised funds to build the Tomb of the Unknown Heroes in Miaoxing Town, Jiangwan. Since construction began in July of the 23rd year of the Republic, the entire project has been completed, and the completion ceremony is scheduled to be held on the 28th of this month. The reporter of the Dagongshe has learned the following information:

Process of Preparation and Construction: During the January 28th Shanghai War in the 21st year of the Republic, a large number of soldiers and civilians in our country were killed. Afterwards, various public organizations in this city and leaders from all walks of life initiated the construction of the Tomb of the Unknown Heroes, so that future generations could admire them. Zhang Gongquan, Zhang Xiaoliang, Du Yuesheng, Liu Hongsheng, Du Chongyuan, Kui Yanfang, Shen Yi, Hu Yunqiu, Dong Dayou, Lin Kanghou, Wang Yansong, and Wang Xiaolai were appointed as construction committee members. The tomb site was surveyed and determined to be in Miaoxing Town, Jiangwan, which belongs to Baoshan County. The tomb site was donated by the Baoshan Shanghai Association, totaling more than 30 mu. However, the location is in the countryside, and the transportation is inconvenient. A road connecting Shanghai was specially built, connecting Lingnan Road in Zhabei to the south and Dachang Town to the west. The entire road was completed in the 23rd year. As for the construction expenses, in addition to the 10,000 yuan donated by the local association, the rest was assisted by important central figures and leaders from all walks of life in Shanghai. The entire project was designed by architect Dong Dayou as a voluntary service, with a total cost of more than 100,000 yuan. After construction began in the 23rd year of the Republic, the entire project was completed in December of last year.

Completion of the Project: The first part of the Tomb of the Unknown Heroes project to be completed was the tomb gate, aisle, surrounding wall, flagpole, stone steps, tombstone, tomb site, and stone coffin (containing the clothes and hats of the deceased). There is a small stream in the middle of the aisle from the gate to the tomb hall, and a bridge has been built. The second phase of the project was the laying of stone steps in front of the hall (using genuine domestic stones), and artificial stones were used around the tomb hall. There are gardens all around. A stone coffin is stored in the tomb hall, with a memorial tablet erected on it. The third phase of the project (i.e., completed at the end of last year) is the Martyrs' Memorial Tower, with miscellaneous items and all the arrangements in the tomb hall. The tombstone was inscribed with the five characters "Tomb of the Unknown Heroes" by Chairman Jiang. The tomb inscription was handwritten by Mr. Zhang Gongquan. Magnificent and imposing, worthy of adoration by future generations.

Completion Ceremony: After the entire project of the tomb was completed, the preparatory committee is now preparing for the completion ceremony. The committee decided to hold the completion ceremony on the anniversary of January 28th because the tomb was established to commemorate January 28th. The reporter of the Dagongshe met with a member of the preparatory committee yesterday. According to him, the completion ceremony of the Tomb of the Unknown Heroes is tentatively scheduled to be held on the 28th of this month. However, whether or not to invite all walks of life at that time, and what kind of ceremony will be held, still needs to be discussed and decided by the preparatory committee.

Wu Fugui Murdered to Death on New Year's Eve: Three Thugs Arrived Suddenly: Five Gunshots to the Body Proved Fatal: Eighty Yuan for What? 124

Wu Fugui, a native of Yancheng, 29 years old, lived in a thatched house in East Dapu Road and made a living by pulling carts. Unfortunately, he was murdered on New Year's Eve at around 12:00 AM. Three thugs suddenly came in, one wearing a gray robe, one wearing an overcoat, and one wearing blue cloth shirt and pants. At that time, Wu was already asleep. The one wearing the overcoat shined a flashlight on him and identified him. Then the one wearing blue cloth pulled out a gun and fired three shots. Wu, being strong and brave, did not fall to the ground. He fired four more shots before hitting him. Two shots hit the head, one in the forehead, with the bullet exiting from the ear, and one in the lip, with the bullet exiting from the back of the neck. One shot hit the abdomen, with the bullet exiting from the back. One shot hit the right leg and one shot hit the left arm, totaling five shots to the body, which proved fatal. At that time, Hu Jueming, the police officer at the nearby post No. 82, heard the alarm and went to pursue the thugs, but they had already escaped. The police officer reported to the Liyuan Road Police Station, which in turn reported to the West Gate Branch, requesting the arrest of the murderer. The local保 informed the court for an autopsy. Subsequently, the deceased's sister-in-law, Wu Wang, came to the case and testified that her younger uncle had pulled a car for Zhou Bu Kui, a Chinese detective in the French Concession police station, but he had resigned more than two months ago. Recently, he had been sick and not doing business. She heard her younger uncle say that he had 80 yuan that he did not send, and that he would make them look good. She didn't know what money it was. After the court examined the body, in addition to filling out the death certificate and ordering the local善堂 to prepare a coffin for burial, they ordered the arrest of the murderer for interrogation.

Xu Axi (27 years old, from Wuxi), an apprentice at the Zhenxingguan Dim Sum Shop at No. 390 Zhejiang Road, slept in the shop hall with four other apprentices the night before last. Unexpectedly, the gas pipe that was installed more than 20 years ago by the Shanghai Gas Company in the alley behind the shop suddenly burst, causing gas to rush into the shop hall. Xu and the others were all poisoned by the coal gas in their sleep and lost consciousness. It was not until around 7:00 AM the next morning that Qin Panquan, the old steward of the shop, discovered it and reported it to the Laozha Patrol Room, ordering the detectives to investigate. An ambulance was called and Xu and the others were rushed to Renji Hospital for treatment. However, Xu died because he had been poisoned too deeply and the rescue was ineffective. The detectives then carried Xu's body to the Fielun Road Coroner's Office. Yesterday morning, Song Genshan, the prosecutor of the First Special District Local Court, along with forensic doctor Zhang Yan and clerk Wang Zuyi, came to the office and confirmed the identity of the body. They then ruled that the deceased Xu Axi had died of coal gas poisoning during his lifetime. The body was handed over to his cousin, Huang Aji, for burial after signing a guarantee. It was also learned that several apprentices in a barber shop at No. 394 next door also suffered from the same poisonous gas.

Changming Electrical Company Suffers a Loss: A Major Blow to the Domestic Goods Industry 129

Changming Company, located at No. 10, Lane 611, Chengdu Road, was established in the spring of 1930. Initially, it manufactured Sanguang brand flashlights, pocket electric heaters, and machine parts. Later, recognizing the popularity of foreign clocks in the domestic market, the company decided to switch to manufacturing Sanguang brand clocks, hoping to stem the outflow of money. They made every effort to use domestic raw materials, machinery, steel molds, and lathes. After more than two years of dedicated research and numerous trials and improvements, the clocks were finally launched. They quickly gained popularity nationwide, making the company a leading force in the domestic clock industry. With the government's implementation of legal tender and the soaring exchange rates, orders poured in. Despite working day and night, they still struggled to meet the demand. Unexpectedly, at around 4 a.m. yesterday, a fire broke out in the western section of the factory, burning for over two hours. All of their assets were destroyed in the blaze. The company's losses amount to no less than 200,000 yuan, a significant loss for the domestic goods industry. The company's management is currently meticulously planning for all necessary follow-up measures. They intend to persevere and restore the company to its original state as quickly as possible, while also striving for expansion to achieve their original goal of reclaiming lost interests.

Public Security Bureau Plans Annual Reduction of Opium Addicts After Deadline for Registration, Aiming to Eradicate Opium Addiction Within a Set Timeframe, While Simultaneously Intensifying Crackdown Efforts 132

The Municipal Public Security Bureau's registration of opium addicts has concluded at the end of last year. This year will mark the start of searches, arrests, and rehabilitation, making the anti-opium work increasingly intensive. The Dagongshe reporter has gathered the following details for your information:

Compiling Statistics, Planning Gradual Reduction. The purpose of the Public Security Bureau's registration of opium addicts is to ascertain the exact number of opium addicts in this city, to formulate a plan for their gradual reduction, thereby eradicating opium addiction. Now that the registration of opium addicts has concluded, detailed statistics should be compiled regarding the number of opium addicts, their ages, addresses, the amount of opium they consume, and the deadlines for their rehabilitation. A special register should be created to facilitate the calculation of daily opium consumption reduction and the verification of deadlines. The Bureau's Opium Addict Registration Section has been compiling these statistics for days. This task is time-consuming due to the number of registered addicts exceeding 37,000. It is expected to be completed by the end of this month. After the statistics are compiled, a plan for annual gradual reduction will be formulated, aiming to eradicate opium addiction within a set timeframe.

Discussing Measures, Intensifying Crackdown. The Bureau acknowledges the enthusiastic participation in the registration of opium addicts. However, some stubborn individuals still refuse to register. The Bureau can no longer tolerate such individuals and will intensify crackdown efforts. Last month, over 3,000 opium addicts were arrested in crackdown operations. Crackdown efforts will be further intensified moving forward. In addition to the Public Security Bureau sending official letters to the Shanghai Municipal Council and the French Concession Police Department for assistance at any time, Mr. Dai, the section chief of the Opium Addict Registration Section, convened a meeting yesterday afternoon with Mr. Zhou Peisan, the head of the Crackdown Unit, and others to discuss measures for intensifying the crackdown. In addition to the decision to reward informants, various other measures were also discussed.

Opium Rehabilitation Hospitals to be Established by a Deadline. Since the Public Security Bureau's registration of opium addicts ended, over 14,000 people who were unable to register have applied for rehabilitation. In addition to the 3,161 people who have already been sent for rehabilitation and the 2,696 people who have successfully quit, over 10,000 people are waiting to be sent for rehabilitation. With the intensification of crackdown efforts, the number of people requiring rehabilitation will inevitably increase. The establishment of a new opium rehabilitation hospital in the city center is urgently needed. According to an official in charge of preparations at the Public Health Bureau, the new opium rehabilitation hospital is now fully equipped, with a capacity of 1,000 people. It was originally scheduled to be established on the 5th, but due to minor incomplete equipment and personnel selection, the opening has been postponed to the 16th of this month, with no further delays expected.

He also presented two official documents from the Zhejiang Provincial Government, dated November 1934, regarding the YiWu County Government's arrest of red pill offender Wang Ronggui and others, who confessed to purchasing red pills from Ye Zicai, requesting Ye's arrest. The detectives brought Wang and Hu to the court for confrontation. Ye Zicai denied entrusting Wang and Hu to transport drugs, and, claiming that he had been residing in the French Concession for many years, opposed the transfer. Lawyer Ge Zhitan defended him. Judge Xiong, upon reviewing the evidence, deemed the evidence complete and ruled that Ye Zicai would be transferred to the Shanghai Municipal Public Security Bureau for questioning. Ye was dissatisfied and filed an appeal, which was rejected by the High Third Branch Court, upholding the original ruling. The case file was returned to the Special No. 2 Court for execution. Upon receiving the case file, the Special No. 2 Court notified the Shanghai Municipal Public Security Bureau, which dispatched detectives to the Special No. 2 Court yesterday morning to transfer Ye. At 10:30 am, Judge Xiong personally went to the Second Criminal Court, instructed the police to bring Ye Zicai from the detention center, and after questioning his name and background, ordered that Ye Zicai be handed over to the officers from the Shanghai Municipal Public Security Bureau for questioning.

Chen Tianyuan and Zhang Arong Guilty of Exchanging Silver Dollars for Profit, Charging Eight and Six Cents per Dollar 134

Chen Tianyuan (44 years old), a Fujianese residing at No. 2, Zhoushanli, Zhoushan Road, conspired with Zhang Arong (who has already been arrested by the Municipal Public Security Bureau) at around 3 pm on December 23rd of last year to sell 812 silver dollars at a certain address in Mengjiang Lane, Wusong Road, exchanging currency to profit from the price difference. He was arrested by the Huishan Police Station. Yesterday morning, he was sent to the First Special District Court. Shanghai Municipal Council lawyer Zhang Shizhu explained the case, stating that the silver dollars came from two employees of a cigarette paper shop who specialized in such illegal activities. The buyer had a disagreement with the sellers over the premium price, and the transaction fell through. The suspects then stole 212 silver dollars. He requested the court to extend the detention period in accordance with Articles 2 and 5 of the Provisional Regulations on Smuggling Common Silver Coins for profit. When questioned, Chen Tianyuan confessed to knowing Zhang Arong for many years. He admitted that he had brought the silver coins and entrusted Shi Wenxiang to negotiate the price. The old silver coins were exchanged for a premium of eight cents per dollar, and the new silver coins for six cents per dollar. However, the transaction was canceled due to an argument. He gave conflicting answers to other questions. Judge Xiao Xiefei ordered him to remain in custody for further questioning in seven days.

Strange Death of Shoe Store Apprentice Zhang Shunbao: Blood from Nostrils, No Shoes on Feet 135

Zhang Shunbao, a 17-year-old from Zhenjiang, was an apprentice at a shoe store in the French Concession. The night before last, Zhang went to the home of Wu Futting, the owner of the shoe store at No. 1, Yonghaili, in the city for dinner and then left to return to the store. However, he suddenly collapsed at the entrance of Yonghaili. It was not until around 9 pm that Tang Luheng, a police officer from the No. 9 post of the Laobeimen Police Station, discovered him while patrolling. Upon closer inspection, the deceased had blood flowing from his nostrils and was not wearing shoes. The death appeared strange. Patrol Officer Zhang Lantian of the police station led officers to conduct a thorough investigation. They summoned Wu Futting's wife, Yang, for questioning. As the case involved a human life, the local headman was instructed to report to the District Court for an autopsy. The police were also dispatched for further investigation to determine the truth.

Fire Extinguishing Foam and Other Items to be Transported as Ordinary Goods Due to Being Non-Hazardous 138

The Beijing-Shanghai, Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Administration received instructions from the Ministry of Railways, stating that the ministry had approved the inclusion of fire extinguishing foam, fire extinguishing powder, fire extinguishing powder cylinders, and filled fire extinguishing powder cylinders in the list of hazardous goods that could be transported from 50 kilograms. The Zhen Dan Machinery and Iron Factory submitted a report stating that some of these goods were not hazardous. After verification, this was found to be true. The Ministry of Railways approved the transport of fire extinguishing foam, fire extinguishing powder, and fire extinguishing powder cylinders as ordinary goods to facilitate sales, effective January 1, 1936. In addition to the approval, the administration was instructed to comply and report accordingly. The administration has forwarded the instructions to the Traffic Department for compliance.

Since the commencement of the clearance sale of inventory at the Nanjing Road headquarters store on December 20th of last year, results have been quite favorable. On that day, revenue was over 6,000 yuan, 4,000 yuan on the second day, and has been consistently over 2,000 yuan every day since then. The revenue is collected by representatives from the Zhengze Accounting Firm, appointed by the creditors, who are stationed in the store. The original employees are only responsible for selling goods. The current liquidation is scheduled for three months. Whether or not it will be continued will be decided at a meeting of the creditors. The dispensary's assets and liabilities are approximately 1 million yuan, and the inventory is valued at over 600,000 yuan. The dispensary also has a branch opposite the Jing'an Temple, which is reportedly scheduled to begin liquidation and clearance sales in mid-February.

Report on the Third National Congress of the Chinese Medical Association 143

The Chinese Medical Association held its Third National Congress on New Year's Day at the Dengtuomo Hotel on Ningbo Road. Over two hundred delegates from dozens of locations including Nanjing attended. The presidium consisted of Qian Longzhang, Ye Jubo, Zhang Kelun, Lu Jimin, Sun Zijie. The opening ceremony began at 10 a.m. (performing the rituals). Chairman Lu Jimin gave a report, stating that the association had been established in 1929, and seven years had passed in a flash. Members in various locations may not be clear about the association's work and activities, which inevitably leads to difficulties in the association's affairs. However, despite being constrained by the environment, the association has continued to work hard. In addition, although it has not made much contribution to national medical construction and social health, it has done its best to promote them gradually. The delegates from various locations have arrived at the third congress, and there are many proposals that will benefit the strength of the nation and the health of the people. He hoped that everyone would discuss them carefully and work hard to implement them. The presidium members Qian Longzhang, Zhang Kelun, and Sun Zijie then delivered speeches. At noon, there was a break for lunch. The delegates Liu Songshi from Guangdong, Zhang Guowei from Nanhui, Hong Xichun from Wuxi, Ni Genghua from Zhenhai, Zhu Bin from Suzhou, Zhang Hong, and others then expressed their opinions. This was followed by a discussion of the following proposals. Wu Yilian and Wang Ziao, members from Suzhou, proposed that the government should universally issue physician licenses. The resolution was: (A) to organize a delegation to petition the government in Nanjing on February 2nd, requesting that those who opened practices before 1929 be naturally issued licenses, and to request relief for those who opened practices after 1929; (B) to collect statistics on the number of people who have not received licenses to concentrate talent. The Shanghai branch proposed the establishment of a New Medical Construction Association by the central government to research and promote new medicine. The resolution was: to request the central government's highest authority to convene national new medical organizations to jointly organize it. A request to the government to establish more public maternity hospitals to benefit the poor was approved, and it was resolved to request the Executive Yuan and the Ministry of Health to order local health administrative agencies to establish them quickly. The Suzhou members requested the Standing Committee to restrict hospitals from indiscriminately admitting students in the future. The resolution was: to submit the matter to the Executive Yuan, the Ministry of Education, the Ministry of Interior, and the Ministry of Health for handling. By this time, it was dusk, and a break was announced for dinner. The discussion of proposals continued at 10 a.m. on the second morning, with presidium members Sun Zijie, Lu Jimin, Qian Longzhang, and Ye Jubo taking turns as chairmen. The resolutions are recorded as follows: The Wuxi members proposed expanding various publications to popularize new medical knowledge. The resolution was that the current executive committee would design and implement it. Xi Yan, a delegate from Chongming, proposed expanding recruitment of members to concentrate new medical talent. The resolution was to design recruitment and notify local branches to encourage members to introduce them as much as possible. There were many other motions regarding the development of association affairs (omitted). After lunch, the second election was held. The list of elected members is recorded as follows: (Executive Committee) Zhang Kelun, Qian Longzhang, Ye Jubo, Ni Genghua, Yao Juyan, Lu Jimin, Dong Weiling, Wang Yuqing, Tu Qihua, Yao Zuodun, Liu Songshi, Liu Renfu, Wan Shaoyun, Zhang Guowei, Sun Yucheng (Alternates) Zhu Bin, Feng Zhiyin, Lai Gongliang, Huang Aihua, Wang Juying, Lu Yunrui, Hong Xichun (Supervisory Committee) Zhang Youmin, Yao Zhicheng, Dai Baocheng (Alternates) Dai Songnian, Hu Zhixiang. Finally, a group photo was taken, and the meeting was adjourned after dinner.

Pudong Electric Company Revises Business Charter, Reduces Electricity Prices 144

To alleviate the burden on users and promote widespread electricity usage, the Pudong Electric Company has revised its business charter and changed its billing system, reducing various electricity prices. This has been submitted to the Shanghai Municipal Public Utilities Bureau, which in turn submitted it to the Municipal Government for approval by the Construction Committee. It will take effect this month. The newly revised prices are as follows:

Electricity Prices: For monthly consumption up to 500 kilowatt-hours, the price is 0.20 yuan per kilowatt-hour. For consumption exceeding 500 kilowatt-hours but not exceeding 1,000 kilowatt-hours, the price for the excess is 0.16 yuan per kilowatt-hour. For consumption exceeding 1,000 kilowatt-hours but not exceeding 3,000 kilowatt-hours, the price for the excess is 0.14 yuan per kilowatt-hour. For consumption exceeding 3,000 kilowatt-hours but not exceeding 5,000 kilowatt-hours, the price for the excess is 0.10 yuan per kilowatt-hour. For consumption exceeding 5,000 kilowatt-hours but not exceeding 15,000 kilowatt-hours, the price for the excess is 0.07 yuan per kilowatt-hour. For consumption exceeding 15,000 kilowatt-hours, the price for the excess is 0.06 yuan per kilowatt-hour. Electricity heating prices: For monthly consumption up to 500 kilowatt-hours, the price is 0.055 yuan per kilowatt-hour. For consumption exceeding 500 kilowatt-hours but not exceeding 1,000 kilowatt-hours, the price for the excess is 0.05 yuan per kilowatt-hour. For consumption exceeding 1,000 kilowatt-hours but not exceeding 3,000 kilowatt-hours, the price for the excess is 0.045 yuan per kilowatt-hour. For consumption exceeding 3,000 kilowatt-hours, the price for the excess is 0.04 yuan per kilowatt-hour.

Power Prices: For monthly average electricity consumption per horsepower up to 50 kilowatt-hours, the price is 0.06 yuan per kilowatt-hour. For consumption exceeding 50 kilowatt-hours but not exceeding 150 kilowatt-hours, the price for the excess is 0.055 yuan per kilowatt-hour. For consumption exceeding 150 kilowatt-hours but not exceeding 250 kilowatt-hours, the price for the excess is 0.04 yuan per kilowatt-hour. For consumption exceeding 250 kilowatt-hours but not exceeding 350 kilowatt-hours, the price for the excess is 0.03 yuan per kilowatt-hour. For consumption exceeding 350 kilowatt-hours, the price for the excess is 0.025 yuan per kilowatt-hour. This power price only applies to users with electric motors of 50 horsepower or less. For users with electric motors of more than 50 horsepower, they can negotiate special favorable rates with the company.

Curing Pulmonary Tuberculosis: The key lies in vigorous physiological defense mechanisms. To achieve a cure for pulmonary tuberculosis, one must first understand how the lesions of pulmonary tuberculosis are naturally cured. This is a very important question, and patients must investigate it. According to what is seen in theory, when tubercle bacillus invades the lung, it multiplies and develops, producing toxins. The lung tissue then undergoes pathological changes, and a small transparent object appears. Over time, it turns yellow and becomes as large as a millet grain. Over time, it gradually expands and becomes a hard lump (this is the lesion). At this time, the tissue cells in the human body exert their natural ability to resist it with all their strength, surrounding and blocking it, so as to stop the pathological changes. This is the physiological defense mechanism in living organisms, and in short, it is natural healing power. The waxing and waning of this defense mechanism determines the victory or defeat of the war between the body and the bacteria. If the defense power is strong, a very strong substance called connective tissue will grow around the lesion, forming a fortress to confine the lesion and completely stop its activity, eventually stopping it completely, leading to a cure. If the defense power is insufficient, the natural healing power will be reduced, and the body will be defeated by the bacteria. As a result, the disease will continue to be active, the symptoms will gradually worsen, and it will become incurable. From this point of view, whether lung disease can be cured depends on the strength of the physiological defense power. There is no doubt about it.

For example, if you break a branch of a plant, it will sprout again at that place; if you damage the skin of an animal, it will form a scar at that place and heal. From this point of view, the treatment of lung disease is based on the principles of curing tuberculosis in modern times, and the experimental reports of clinical physicians, "Lung Vital" Phith Weal is indeed the most reasonable and well-founded hormone preparation. Prevention of Hemoptysis 152

— Shen Zhaoquan

The source of hemoptysis. There are about two kinds. One is bleeding when the tracheal branch point membrane is damaged. One is bleeding from rupture of blood vessels in lung tuberculosis cavities. The former is common in severe bronchitis, whooping cough, etc. when coughing severely. The latter is true lung tuberculosis hemoptysis. However, pulmonary paragonimiasis, lung abscess (i.e., lung suppurative), bronchial dilatation, lung syphilis, etc. also have symptoms of hemoptysis.

Lung tuberculosis cavities. Different sizes. When microvessels rupture in extremely small cavities. Cause small hemoptysis. Such as blood spots or blood streaks in coughed up sputum. When relatively large blood vessels rupture in large cavities. It causes large hemoptysis.

All cavities are mostly in communication with the trachea. Therefore, it is more difficult to stop bleeding. This is because the free end of the ruptured blood vessel in the cavity. There is no chance to compress and stop bleeding.

Although there is a lot of hemoptysis. But there are very few who die directly from hemoptysis. And the blood clot. Blocks the trachea. Therefore, dying of suffocation is common.

The cause of hemoptysis. It is that the blood vessels undergo tuberculous changes. As a result, it ruptures. And mental agitation, or physical fatigue and cough are the causes.

Prevention of hemoptysis. It is impossible to prevent hemoptysis at the onset of the disease. If there is a violent cough. Then always try to remove it. Those with hemoptysis during the course of the disease. Often caused by excessive force. As a result, blood vessels rupture. Therefore, the prevention method. That is, no matter what kind of action. Always pay attention. Never use too much force. Anyone who has been diagnosed by a doctor as having early lung disease. You must engage in recuperation. Strictly abide by the health regimen.

Recently used drugs to prevent hemoptysis. The efficacy of organ preparations is very great. Such as those made from hormones extracted from lungs and spleen. "Lung Vital" Phith Weal is particularly effective. If there is stubborn hemoptysis. Blood spots or blood streaks are often found in the sputum. In addition to strictly observing the health regimen. Taking "Lung Vital" Phith Weal can achieve recovery.

Children's Educational Novel

Little Men (I) (IV) (II) 184

— Original by Louisa M. Alcott, translated by Zheng Xiaocang

"Maybe a beggar slept over there and stole it," Nat suggested, offering an opinion.

Amy thought that Nat's words did not make sense. She said, "Mr. Laurie manages things very strictly. Besides, beggars wouldn't look for money in that old threshing machine."

"Could it be Mr. Laurie himself?" Jack said.

"Oh, no! Old Laurie is as bright as the clear sky. We would never encounter him taking even a penny from us," said, clearing his beloved friend of all suspicion.

Little Qiao then said, "Whoever took it, let's say it early, don't wait for people to find out," saying so with a serious expression, as if a great disaster had befallen their family.

"I know you think I took it," Ned couldn't help but shout, his face flushed red and his expression very nervous.

Lang said, "Only know where it is."

"I happened to be there—but I didn't take it. I tell you I didn't! I didn't!" Ned shouted in desperation. At this time, Mr. Fei walked in and quickly shouted, "Easy, easy, my child! What are you making a fuss about?"

Children's Special

Please Children, Establish a New Patriotic Aspiration 185

— Qiulang

The New Year of the 25th year of the Republic of China has arrived. You should be so happy to have food and play during this great New Year! And the schools have a vacation, allowing you to be free and do whatever you want. You are little angels in paradise, which is so enviable!

However, our country is now facing internal and external troubles, and the country is in dire straits! To save the country from danger, revive the nation, and avenge our humiliation and strive for strength, although it is the responsibility of adults, you children are the future masters of the country. Therefore, it can be said that you have a certain responsibility, and you must establish a new patriotic aspiration from this year. Even in the happy New Year, you must not forget the national crisis! You must carefully study all kinds of knowledge, listen carefully to the teachings of teachers, and follow the guidance of fathers and brothers. Have courage, perseverance, and diligence. Do not be lazy, do not lie, and do not be superstitious. These are all the initial preparations for becoming the masters of the country. In the future, you can serve the society and the country. This is a small opinion, and I hope that our dear children will adopt it!

The Year of the Rat Talk About Rats 186

— Da Zhai

This year is the Year of the Rat. Let's talk to the children about rats: Bad people are called "rat-like fellows." Children should aspire to be people who are beneficial to society and the country. All "rat-thieving" behaviors should be avoided, so as not to be regarded by others as the most repulsive rat.

Cowardly people are called "as timid as a mouse." If people lack courage, they cannot act bravely when they should. They are called useless cowards. If a small, weak country like Aguo confronts a powerful one for so long, can it do so without courage? This is currently a proportional example. But being bold cannot mean recklessness, so the idiom says: "Have the courage of a lion, but the carefulness of a serpent."

People without resolve are called "hesitating between two opinions." This kind of mentality often causes one to miss good opportunities, which cannot be recovered. For example, children, in this golden age, are unwilling to make up their minds to study hard, and year after year, they make no progress. Then, "If you don't work hard when you are young, you will regret it when you are old." It will be too late to regret in the future. At the beginning of this new year, you must make up your mind.

A bubonic plague transmitted by fleas parasitizing on rats is called "rat plague." If this disease is discovered, it spreads extremely fast and causes many deaths. However, children, if you see others behaving badly and follow their example, when you are infected with bad habits and assimilated, it is truly "one who dwells near vermin is verminous." It is as dangerous as the rat plague spreading, at worst leading to personal ruin and disgrace, and in extreme cases, harming one's life. Therefore, you must not blindly follow when others do bad things.

Although rats are small things, some people use them to perform on the street, called "rat shows." Rats can be trained to perform and earn money. Children, if you have no skills, isn't this "being inferior to a rat"? Year of the Rat, Year of the Rat! How should you strive for progress?

New Vigor 188

— Chen Liang

On New Year's Day, Miss Shan got up very early. The sun shone in from outside the window, making the pot of daffodils on the table exceptionally green and upright. The small fruits of the nandina appeared even more vividly red, and the singing of the lark under the eaves was more melodious than usual. It seemed that there was a new atmosphere and new vigor before her eyes.

How happy Miss Shan was! She changed into new lake-green clothes, and asked her sister to pin a sprig of crabapple near her temples. She didn't apply powder or rouge, as she already had healthy, apple-colored cheeks. She was very busy going back and forth, and the little kitten followed her feet, as if helping with the work. It turned out that Miss Shan had planned to invite a few children to dinner on New Year's Day. The dishes were prepared by her sister, and the candy plate and decorations were arranged by herself.

The first guest to arrive was Li Shunfu, wearing a washed and cleaned calico shirt. He was the son of a tailor and came from a poor family, but Miss Shan always treated him very well because he loved cleanliness, was disciplined, and polite. At this moment, when they met, they bowed to each other, and Miss Shan led him to sit in the specially decorated guest room. The ceiling was covered with bright national flags and paper streamers, and the walls were covered with Miss Shan's handicrafts and crayon drawings. There were three vases of fresh flowers on the rectangular table.

After a while, Wang Dabao came, Huang Lifen came, Zhu Agui, Chen Manman, Zhang Renlin... also came. Everyone sat around eating candy and talking about what they did at home on New Year's Eve. Miss Shan then led all the children to sing the national anthem of the Republic of China, and asked her sister to play the organ. Then, she went upstairs to invite her mother down and introduced her to the guests. All the guests stood up and bowed respectfully. They sat down again and listened quietly to the speech:

"New Year's Day is originally a festival for children. Today, I am very happy to see you gathering together lovingly. I hope you will always be so loving, and when you grow up, you will still be on good terms. You should not be divided by wealth or status. Everyone should help each other, encourage each other, not learn from the inferior, not be lazy, be good children, and when you grow up, be sound good citizens, love your compatriots, love your country, and love the peaceful people of the world. Today, you can have as much fun as you want, but in the midst of happiness, don't forget that there are still many children suffering from hunger and cold!" After Miss Shan's mother finished speaking, it was time to eat. Everyone was very orderly.

The room was filled with a new atmosphere and new vigor. The national flag seemed exceptionally bright and radiant.

A Visit to a Children's Sports Meet 189

— Ba Ling

The Shanghai County Minhang Public Education Center, in order to encourage children's interest in sports and to attract the attention of people in society to children's lives, held a children's sports meet on New Year's Day this year. On this day, the reporter also went to visit. Although the weather was not very good, there were still more than 80 children participating, which cannot but be said to be a good achievement!

This children's sports meet was divided into two groups, A and B. Group A had seven events: kicking shuttlecock, jump rope, archery, basketball, rolling iron hoop, obstacle race, and air gun target shooting. Group B had four events: kicking shuttlecock, archery, and rolling iron hoop. Some events had to be held on the sports field, and some could be held in the hall of the center. This decision was made because the drizzle in the sky was intermittent, so the interest was naturally affected to a considerable extent. However, the spirit of the children was still very enthusiastic, so the center, in order to adapt to the needs of the environment, changed some of the sports that could be held indoors to be held indoors, such as racing, air gun target shooting, archery, basketball, etc., which would have to be held when the weather was clear!

The supplies for this children's sports meet were all provided by the center. At the same time, a lot of prizes were prepared, such as books, stationery, towels, toothbrushes, toothpaste, handkerchiefs, toys, food, etc., which were prepared to be awarded to children with excellent results. This spirit of promoting children's sports is really admirable.

The happiness of children is now being widely noticed by adults! I also hope that public education institutions in various places will promote and reward it as much as possible within their capabilities.

Kaleidoscope of the World 190

— Ren

The Republic of Grapes—Portugal

The Terrain of Portugal The Flag of Portugal

The Cork Trees of Portugal The Capital, Lisbon

The Women of Portugal The Men of Portugal

A Fallen Family Portugal, like our China, used to be a powerful country, but now its national strength is far from what it used to be. It lives quietly in a corner of Western Europe. Its territory is small, its population is small, revolutions and riots occur every year, people's livelihood is difficult, and national debt is piled up. Although it still has vast territories, its foundation is shaky, like a wealthy family that has fallen into decline. Although the frame is large, the content is empty, and it cannot avoid being laughed at by its neighbors as a "fallen family."

A Patterned National Flag The national flag of Portugal is: The entire surface is divided into red and green, green on the left, red on the right, and green is narrower than red. In the middle is a yellow circular pattern. (Two)

The Terrain is Like a Cloth Sail Portugal is located at the southwestern tip of Europe. It is bordered by Spain on the northeast and the Atlantic Ocean on the southwest. The Azores and Madeira archipelagos in northwestern Africa are also its directly affiliated territories. The terrain is long and narrow, quite like a cloth sail raised on a sailboat. (One)

Sanatorium for Lung Diseases The capital of Portugal, Lisbon, is located in the western part of the country, with beautiful scenery and a very good climate. People with lung diseases from various countries mostly live here to recuperate. (Four)

Many Vineyards Portugal is an agricultural country. Vineyards account for 35% of the country's land. They also have a famous product, which is cork stoppers. These cork stoppers are made from the bark of cork trees. After a layer of bark is peeled off, a new layer will grow in eight or nine years. Portugal and Spain account for 70% of the world's cork stoppers. (Three)

Men and Women The temperament of the Portuguese is very frivolous, they love vanity, like to enjoy themselves, and do not seek to improve. Education is not yet universal, and there are many people without knowledge in the lower classes of society. We can know what their clothes are like by looking at (Figure 5) and (Figure 6).

The yarn market opened yesterday, and the trend remains firm. This is because the sales of spot yarn are becoming more active. Tuesday, December 31st: U.S. cotton opened, and the trend was firm due to short covering in the near month. Only two delivery notices for the January contract were issued, and there was a lack of new accounts. Colleagues were watching. The market situation was mixed in the afternoon. Colleagues bought the near month, and shorts shifted from near to distant months. Finally, due to rumors that the government had stopped issuing notices, there was a lot of short covering in January and March. As a result, spot prices rose by 15 points, near-month prices rose by 8 to 18 points, and distant-month prices fell by 3 to 8 points. British spot cotton fell by 4 points, and futures fell by 1 point. Indian cotton rose due to firm silver prices and short covering and speculative buying. European exporters sold slightly. Grade List for June Bidding Yarn and Cotton: Two New Grades Added to Cotton Fine绒, Cotton Yarn Changed to Bi-Monthly Inspections 201

The Chinese Yarn and Cloth Exchange held a cotton appraisal meeting on December 30th for the purpose of delivery in June of the 25th year. As a result of the appraisal, two new grades were added to the first grade. The original four types of A, B, C, and D were Lingbao cotton, Luoyang cotton, Tianjin American cotton, and Shandong American cotton, which were four grades. Now, Nanyuan cotton, Chaoyi cotton, Beihe cotton, Zhangde cotton, and Weinan cotton are newly added to the second grade. In the second grade, Baiwan cotton and Qiyang cotton are added as two grades. The remaining third and fourth grades have not been changed and are the same as the May grades. The audited and modified procedure grade prices are listed below for reference.

Furthermore, a cotton yarn appraisal meeting was convened on December 26th for the review of the two-month delivery substitutes for June and July of the 25th year. As a result, only the 20-count Jin Shuangxi brand produced by Shenxin No. 6 Factory was added, and the grades of the remaining 20-count, 16-count, and 10-count remained unchanged and were the same as in May. It was found that the bidding yarn grade inspection grades were previously inspected monthly, but from the June period of the 25th year onwards, they will be changed to bi-monthly inspections, it is said.

Delusional Disorder 209

— Editor

Delusion is one of the symptoms of mental disorders. Its types include delusional jealousy, imaginary delusions, hallucinatory delusions, emotional delusions, grandiose delusions, and logical delusions, which are distinguished by their content. There are also grandiose delusions, delusions of guilt, delusions of insignificance, delusions of terror, and delusions of persecution.

Delusion is the judgment of error and false belief. There are three characteristics: The content of the delusion is impossible and absurd. The content of the delusion is inconsistent with the level of education and the circumstances of the environment. Although the content of the delusion is a false belief, the patient has extremely strong confidence.

If this condition is not treated early, the delusion will become increasingly delusional and extremely dangerous. Initially, it will not only lose its proper soundness.
