Current Affairs Research

The Lifespan of the Laval Cabinet 222

— Shouhe

Due to the development of the economic panic and the deepening of the financial crisis, the turbulence of French politics in recent years can be said to be more serious than that of any other country. In the past, most French cabinets collapsed within a few months, and some even died within two or three days of taking office. From this situation alone, it is conceivable how unstable the French political situation has been in recent years. Under such an unstable political situation, it has promoted the development of French political thought at both the left and right extremes and the sharpening of the struggle between the two. In fact, right-wing organizations in France, such as the Croix-de-Feu, composed of veteran soldiers, already have more than 300,000 members, and the Jeunesses Patriotes also have more than 325,000 members. In addition, organizations such as Action Française also have many members. At the same time, on the other hand, various left-wing parties in France, such as the Radical Socialist Party, the Socialist Party, and the Communist Party, also have great strength. As a result, direct conflicts between the left and right extremes can be seen in places such as Paris almost at any time; moreover, various right-wing factions have formed a united organization to act in unison, and various left-wing parties have also united to form a "Popular Front" to confront the right-wing alliance. In this way, France, the so-called last bastion of democratic politics, is increasingly showing that it is difficult to maintain the lifespan of this democratic politics.

The Laval cabinet can be said to have emerged and been preserved in the struggle between the left and right extremes in France. However, due to the development of this struggle between the two extremes, the lifespan of the Laval cabinet is also increasingly in danger. In the last two or three months of last year, the Laval cabinet repeatedly encountered difficulties and faced danger several times. It can be said to be extremely fortunate that it has been able to maintain itself until now. Although the Laval cabinet has overcome several difficulties, according to general observation, its position is still not stable, and whether it can extend its lifespan to beyond January is still a big question. In order to examine the fate of the Laval cabinet in the future, it is necessary to review its recent encounters.

In November last year, France experienced a political crisis due to financial issues and the issue of banning the armed organizations of right-wing groups (i.e., the issue of protecting the republican system). When these two issues were raised in the Chamber of Deputies, the left-wing parties demanded that the latter be discussed first, while the government insisted that the former be discussed first. As a result, a conflict occurred, and they were unable to reach an agreement. The result was that many upper-level leaders of the Radical Socialist Party, such as Herriot, supported the Laval government, and the majority of the Chamber of Deputies agreed to discuss the financial issue first, and passed the government's financial plan in the Chamber of Deputies, allowing the Laval cabinet to overcome the first difficulty. As for why some upper-level leaders of the Radical Socialist Party supported the Laval cabinet on this issue, Herriot explained that: "If the current cabinet collapses, there are three possible solutions: one is to organize a 'Popular Front government', which would require dissolving the Chamber of Deputies; the second is for the Radical Party to form a cabinet alone, but under the current circumstances, no one in our party dares to take sole responsibility; the third is to organize a new cabinet similar to the current one, so why bother?" In other words, some upper-level leaders of the Radical Socialist Party are temporarily supporting the Laval cabinet because they are terrified of both the extreme left and the extreme right under the current circumstances, and they have no choice but to do so while wavering. Since then, the Laval cabinet has been able to escape danger time and again, all thanks to the rescue of Herriot and others.

After overcoming the first difficulty, the second difficulty encountered by the Laval cabinet was the issue of banning the armed organizations of right-wing groups. This issue was even more serious than the financial issue, because it was a question of determining victory or defeat on the first line of defense between the left and right sides. The banning of right-wing military organizations was not only strongly advocated by the extreme left, but also demanded by the vast majority of the Radical Socialist Party in the middle. At the same time, the right-wing groups were also unwilling to give in, and there was a great possibility of serious disturbances in places such as Paris. Therefore, Laval felt that the solution to the problem was very difficult and repeatedly delayed the discussion of the issue in order to find an opportunity to get out of danger. Sure enough, when the Chamber of Deputies debated this issue, Socialist leader Blum and Croix-de-Feu leader de la Rocque both stated that they were willing to dissolve the "defense organizations" in their parties. Laval immediately took the opportunity to propose a bill "prohibiting the placement of armed forces in parties." As a result, three bills were passed: The Minister of Interior may, after consulting with the State Council, dissolve military groups that endanger the security of the political system; those who illegally

Page 22

possess weapons will be severely punished; those who publish radical remarks in the press aimed at instigating murder, even if it does not have any effect, their responsible persons may be submitted to the court for punishment. As a result, the Laval cabinet overcame the second difficulty. According to the bills passed by the Chamber of Deputies, Laval could simultaneously ban the armed organizations on both the left and right sides, so his overcoming the second difficulty was precisely a manifestation of his cunning.

However, the Laval cabinet was not stable after overcoming one difficulty after another. What followed was the Chamber of Deputies' discussion of foreign policy; this issue was triggered by the Anglo-French peace plan to resolve the Italian-Ethiopian War. After the Anglo-French peace plan was put forward, the world considered it an unfair plan. Whether in Paris, London, Geneva, or various small countries around the world, there was an atmosphere of opposition to this plan, causing the League of Nations under the control of Britain and France to reject this plan and causing British Foreign Secretary Hoare to step down. A similar serious reaction occurred in France. In this reaction, first, Herriot, a minister without portfolio who supported the Laval cabinet, was forced to resign as the leader of the Radical Socialist Party, and then the left-wing parties in the Chamber of Deputies opposed the government's diplomacy, making the fate of the Laval cabinet very dangerous. However, the result was also that a faction of upper-level leaders of the Radical Socialist Party were unwilling to start a cabinet crisis and decided to support the government. After Laval's "tongue-lashing of the Confucian scholars," the cabinet won again.

From the above facts, we can see that the lifespan of the Laval cabinet depends entirely on the support of some upper-level leaders of the Radical Socialist Party. Naturally, the wavering compromise of Socialist leader Blum and others can also be said to be a pillar of the Laval cabinet's existence, but mainly, if it were not for the strong support of Herriot and others, it would have collapsed long ago. We know that the Radical Socialist Party is the largest political party in France and occupies a pivotal position in the parliament. Although it has joined the "Popular Front," some of its leaders, such as Herriot, fear the extreme left more than they fear the extreme right, so they have to temporarily support the "moderate" Laval cabinet. How long the Laval cabinet's lifespan can be extended in the future, needless to say, will be determined by the strength of the Radical Socialist Party's support for it.

Currently, the political views of the French Radical Socialist Party are not unified. Some are increasingly approaching the right wing, while others are gradually moving to the left. If the conflict between the left and right extremes continues to develop in France, a serious division will inevitably occur within the Radical Socialist Party. In fact, the votes of the Radical Socialist Party's members of parliament were very inconsistent in the past parliamentary debates. If events develop to the point where neutral wavering is absolutely not allowed, then Herriot and others will be powerless even if they want to support the Laval cabinet.

Judging from the current situation, Laval is increasingly moving to the right, trying to extend his lifespan under the protection of the right wing and wavering elements. However, due to the unsolvable problem of the franc, the inability to overcome financial difficulties, and the irreconcilable struggle between the left and right extremes, the lifespan of the Laval cabinet is something that no insurance company in the world dares to insure.

If the Laval cabinet collapses, and if extreme politics of the left or right appears in France, the result will have a decisive effect on changes in the international situation.

Weekend Literary Society

Literature and War 223

— Xuqing

War, this is a very extraordinary change in human life. Due to the occurrence of war, all the equilibrium and order of society will be greatly damaged, and the ordinary lives of many groups of people cannot continue to be preserved. Therefore, all social culture cannot continue to adopt the law of gradual change and develop continuously in a normal state. Literature is also the same. In places where war occurs, there must be great changes. In fact, under the constant sound of machine guns, under the bombing of cannons, under the ruined homes, property, and the cries of people with injured bodies, under the symphony of the victor's triumphal songs and the loser's laments, any calm writer, any "surreal" poet, cannot but express their attitude towards war, and cannot but describe the thoughts and feelings of the people around them in the war.

When the World War from 1914 to 1918 occurred, whether in Germany, France, or Britain, all of Europe and even the whole world's literature was affected by the war. General writers created war-related works from their respective standpoints. Many literary researchers have divided modern literature into two stages: pre-war and post-war. This is an obvious fact. Now the world situation has become extremely tense, and everywhere is filled with the smell of gunpowder. No one can say for sure that war will break out tomorrow or the day after tomorrow. Therefore, the changes that will occur in world literature and general culture are absolutely predictable. In order to predict the development and change patterns of literature in the future war, and in order to point out the path that literature should take at that time, we believe that it is necessary to explain the issue of literature and war; especially for the things of the last World War and literature that are closest to us, we must study it in more detail. The reason why we are writing this article is here.

Although war has a great effect on every writer's creation, because each writer's life and world view are different, their feelings about war are also different. For example, in the last World War, writers from all over the world, some were from the standpoint of patriotism to encourage war, some sang the songs of humanitarianism or conservatism in the war, some took the description of people's suffering in the war as their own task, some opposed war and negated everything from the standpoint of extreme individualism, and some actually described the real situation of the war, or even further opposed war from the standpoint of social evolution. In this way, there were a wide variety of them, you name it, we have it, it can be said to be "a dazzling array." Now, in order to understand the problem more clearly, we can also briefly discuss several major literary tendencies in the last World War.

First of all, what deserves our attention is patriotic war literature. According to statistics, in the first year of the outbreak of the war, there were as many as 1.5 million kinds of patriotic poems in Germany alone; the declaration signed by 93 artists and thinkers such as Hauptmann and Döblin and Wassermann, "Why Can't We Not Fight?", is a world-known expression of defending war ideology and militarism. In addition, in countries such as Britain and France, so-called patriotic war literature was also very popular in the early stages of the war, although it was far less fanatical than in Germany. In fact, the banning of Shaw's war satire in Britain at that time, and Romain Rolland's expulsion from France because of his opposition to the war and intolerance by French patriots, the opposite significance of these two things was the high tide of patriotic thought in Britain and France at that time; because if Britain and France were not enthusiastic about patriotism at that time, Shaw and Romain Rolland would not have suffered such treatment.

The second is the tendency of conservatism and humanitarianism that occurred in the war. For example, the humanism represented by Babbitt and More in the United States is a kind of conservatism. They also "oppose" war, and Babbitt himself has specifically protested against the declaration of Hauptmann and others defending the war, but they believe that the cause of the war is due to the excessive development of Rousseau's liberalism and Bacon's scientific thought, so their opposition to war is against material civilization, "overthrowing scientific despotism," and wanting to revive the Eastern "doctrine of the mean" to stabilize the world. This kind of "anti-war" tendency is not to push the world forward, but to try to restore the world to the sixteenth and seventeenth centuries or even the Middle Ages; in the realistic sense, it is used to preserve the conservatism of the real world. As for humanitarian literature, because the war has created a cruel picture of the world, so this is even more popular in the development process of the war, such as Kuprin's "The Garden of the Holy Virgin" in Russia, Lagerlöf's "The Outcast" in Sweden, and even some works by Hauptmann in Germany, can be said to be humanitarian, Ibanez's "The Four Horsemen of the Apocalypse" and "The Mediterranean" in Spain are also sad literary works wearing the cloak of humanitarianism. In his work, there is such a rather pleasant sentence: "Since we are born, everyone has the right to live. The rich, the poor, the strong, the weak, the large, the small, the old, the young, everyone has the right to live. The purpose of our birth is not for others to kill us one day, nor to kill each other, fight each other, and finally kill ourselves. ..." This is a rather touching humanitarian rhetoric.

In addition, in the war and after the end of the war, there are also literary works in the world that express the despair of intellectuals, there are novels and dramas that describe the horror of war and completely oppose war, there are also futurists who shout "Long live the war" and Dadaists who "spit on everything" appear, ... Due to space limitations, we cannot list them all in detail here. However, among them, such as Remarque's "All Quiet on the Western Front" describing the horror of war, Shaw and Rolland and Barbusse's anti-war works are the most influential in the current world literature, and have opened up new paths for war literature, so their works deserve special study by those who study modern world literature or study war literature to read them carefully. In that middle (such as in "All Quiet on the Western Front", in Latzko's "Men in War" and Barbusse's "Under Fire"), you can see the cruel and real pictures of war, and you can also think about how to eliminate war and move towards the path of light. Naturally, there are also many shortcomings in their war literature, such as Shaw's "Killing Instinct", Latzko's absolute "pacifism", and Rolland's humanitarian tendencies, which can be said to be somewhat incorrect. But when we study modern literature, especially when studying war literature, they are still worthy of special attention.

The above is a brief narrative of the issue of the last World War and world literature. Now, the Second World War has become a reality again. Although we cannot say that history will be completely replayed, although we cannot say that the changes that will occur in world literature when a new war occurs will be the same as the changes that occurred in literature in the last World War, we know that human imitation is the strongest. If people living in reality find something that is beneficial to them in the past history, they will definitely follow suit and revive that thing. Therefore, it is not difficult for us to think that when a new war occurs, patriotic literature that defends war, conservatism that fundamentally opposes material civilization due to war, and humanitarianism that cries and begs for mercy for war, all have the possibility of reappearing in new forms. Moreover, in fact, there are now some official intellectuals who are advocating and helping the war of aggression. A very obvious example is Marconi's efforts in the work of aggression in Abyssinia. The futurists who regard war as "the best hygiene" are still enthusiastically welcoming the arrival of the god of war. Once the world war breaks out widely, these official intellectuals do not know how they will dance wildly before the god of war!

If literature is not a pastime, if it still has some effect, then this effect should be to seek welfare for human society at that time. War is cruel, it destroys human life and destroys human life. If literature must undergo great changes in and before the war, then good literature should oppose war and oppose the literature that defends war for the happiness of mankind. But this opposition is not to fundamentally overthrow all material civilization, to make people return to the Middle Ages, that is conservative, and even reversing; this opposition should be standing in a progressive position, actively eliminating the social factors that produce war, so that material civilization can be more highly developed, so that mankind is more happy. At the same time, opposing war is not effective by humanitarian crying and begging for mercy, but to oppose war with the power to fundamentally eliminate war. For example, the wars of colonial and semi-colonial countries for independence and liberation are against the imperialists who are the masters of the current world, and therefore are also a progressive war that fundamentally eliminates war. Good literature should support and praise this progressive war. In the war, excellent writers should say to everyone: "The people are fighting for a few people. The few people are - corpse-eating ghosts who get fat from war!" At the same time, excellent writers should also use the power of literature to awaken weak nations and truly anti-war groups to resist those "corpse-eating ghosts who get fat from war" and fundamentally eliminate war.

Outport Postal Agency

The "Old Customer" of the Fresh Goods Depot 224

— Ren

Shenyang Correspondence: Near Shenyang Railway Station, there are over thirty fresh goods depots, accommodating approximately over two thousand "old customers," all stationed here by various merchant firms on a regular basis.

These "old customers," regularly "stationed" at the depots, not only procure goods for their respective stores but also extensively promote and solicit business for their stores' products; their responsibilities are no less burdensome than those of a plenipotentiary ambassador stationed abroad. Their daily work is similar to that of ambassadors and ministers, reporting local market conditions to their stores and employing commercial skills to negotiate with major markets. Therefore, the prosperity and decline of a store's business is entirely in the hands of these "old customers."

Becoming an "old customer" is not easy. Most start as apprentices, requiring extensive commercial experience, proficiency in abacus calculation, skillful eloquence, and a courteous demeanor. Whenever we stroll through the many depots in Toudaogou near the station, we can always see three to five "old customers" with smiling faces (perhaps forced) negotiating deals with customers in courtyards stacked with goods. Their humble attitude makes you want to do business with them immediately.

Most of the people who act as "old customers" here are from Leting, Changli, and Luanzhou. Even in Changchun, those who dominate commerce are mostly their fellow townsmen. Therefore, "old customers" who speak the dialects of Leting, Changli, and Luanzhou have a significant advantage in transactions. However, due to the intrusion of Japanese commercial capital, which has weakened the commercial influence of Leting, Changli, and Luanzhou, these "old fellow townsmen" "old customers" can no longer live as comfortably as before.

As for the private lives of "old customers," they are quite interesting. Although they handle transactions involving millions of dollars annually, it is difficult to find a writing desk in their offices. They conduct business negotiations mostly on mahjong tables or beside opium beds. No matter how large the transaction, it can be decided with a word in such places. Others negotiate in teahouses. Strangely, in Shenyang, playing cards and smoking opium are quite common. Therefore, the daily routine of a typical "old customer" can be divided into two parts. From 8:00 AM to 12:00 PM, they are busy with the abacus, shipping and receiving goods, thoroughly enjoying themselves. After lunch at twelve o'clock, it is time for leisure, which can also be said to be the start of new business negotiations. As soon as the mahjong table is set up in the depot, the "old customers" entering and leaving the depot will sit down without invitation, talking and playing mahjong, discussing everything from world affairs to personal lives, casually leading to serious topics, and then getting down to business. Their deals are all concluded in this casual manner. A large-scale depot has at least a dozen mahjong tables every day, no less than a club. The gambling stakes are also high, but they don't care about losing a little money on mahjong as long as they get a good price for a batch of goods. This only describes a portion of the older "old customers," who, due to their age, are unwilling to move around. There is also a group of young "old customers," whose minds are as numb as those of the older "old customers." Their preference is mostly for prostitutes rather than opium, frequenting brothels.

The salary of an "old customer," generally speaking, is about three to four hundred dollars per year, but no one can say for sure. Because nine out of ten "old customers" engage in some personal trading, there is no fixed rule for how much money they earn each day. Moreover, many "old customers" are themselves bosses, so it is difficult to compile statistics on their income. Furthermore, an "old customer," whether doing export or import business, can always manipulate prices. If the exported goods sell at a high price, they pocket a portion of the profit; if the imported goods are purchased at a low price, they can secretly increase the price. The store gives them full authority and does not interfere. Therefore, if an "old customer" is slightly disloyal to the store, the store will inevitably close down. The longevity of a store is in the hands of the "old customers" stationed abroad.

Timely Articles

### New Year's Message 225

— Shi

Time flies, days and months do not linger. In the blink of an eye, the Republic of China's twenty-fourth year has quietly passed amidst our sighs, laments, moans, and cries. Looking back, we do not know where our tears come from; looking forward, we try to smile but cannot! With national crises looming and human affairs deteriorating, we are filled with a myriad of emotions as the new year begins. Realizing that endless pessimism is of no practical help, we must think about how to resolve ourselves and work diligently in the coming years. Thus, I offer this "New Year's Message."

1. Expectations for Administrative Personnel: The foundation of a nation's politics lies in local autonomy. Therefore, to ensure the stability of the nation's foundation, we must first strive to complete local autonomy. But to achieve local autonomy, we must first train the people. However, it has been more than five years since political tutelage began. Has the work of political tutelage reached perfection without any shortcomings? Can the current officials in charge of political tutelage be said to be blameless before the world? Alas! It is better not to speak, as discussing it inevitably leads to lament. There are many administrative organs and personnel today, but upon closer inspection, some sit idly, wasting resources, signing in under false pretenses, and spending their days in leisure; others bury themselves at their desks, working endlessly on official documents, only knowing "because of this, therefore," and never asking about practical matters, focusing on reimbursement for superiors, earning a living for themselves, deceiving others as a means, and being perfunctory to subordinates, spending their spare time uttering official platitudes to entertain themselves, and when idle, putting on official airs to impress others. With facts like these, the results are predictable. Thus, the people who have been "trained" for so long remain the same year after year, and the local affairs that have been "governed" for so long remain unchanged. Since the engine of political action is a complete mess, the so-called achievements of political tutelage are nothing more than empty talk on paper. With such political tutelage, when will the nation's foundation be laid, and when will the nation have a chance to be saved?

Continued on Page Five

Page 23

Page 24

Page 25

Realizing that governance does not require much talk, and that resolution is paramount in administration, and with national crises escalating and the situation being dire, as we approach the end of the year and welcome the new, learning from past mistakes and deeply regretting past follies, and renewing ourselves with a fresh start for future efforts, for the sake of the nation and the people, we dare to offer our humble advice to all administrative personnel: "Starting from the twenty-fifth year of the Republic of China, please abandon your 'accumulated habits' and 'lethargy,' embrace the vitality and enthusiasm of the New Year, revitalize your spirits, fulfill your missions, delve deep into the people, diligently seek out their grievances, actively carry out both necessary and revolutionary measures, base all internal and external policies on the will of the people, strive for efficiency in political tutelage, avoid formalism, avoid grand displays, abolish slogans and mottos, resolve to work hard diligently, do not deceive yourselves or others, do not be complacent, enter the new year, create a new life, the past is like smoke, useless to talk about, the future is long, let us work together."

2. Expectations for Youth: Youth is the most precious period of life, and vibrant youth is a true reflection of ourselves. Youth is also the backbone of the nation. If a solid foundation is not laid in youth, the edifice of future careers will inevitably be impossible to build upward. But, young people, in this season of renewal, try to examine yourselves in the stillness of the night, can you be without shame before yourselves, your parents, your teachers, and your nation? Of course, there are those who are acutely aware of the importance of individual responsibility and the urgent need for talent in the future of the nation, and who diligently encourage themselves and strive without ceasing, but there are also those who fail to live up to the expectations of their parents and teachers, squandering their parents' hard-earned money, pursuing sensual pleasures, loitering in dance halls, ignorant of science, and getting headaches from books. They are vaguely aware of world affairs, don't care about national affairs, are satisfied with obtaining diplomas, and aim to become high officials after graduation. There are even more of these. May I ask, how can the nation's hope be placed on such people? If the life of our dying nation does not perish in their hands, when will it perish?

Oh, our youth, as brilliant as the morning sun! At this juncture, may I not offer a word of sincere advice? I say: "The past cannot be undone, but the future can still be pursued. From the twenty-fifth year of the Republic of China, determine your bright outlook on life, recognize your correct path, cultivate your progressive thoughts, and strive with all your might for the people, the nation, the family, and yourselves, and step onto the great path of life. To save the nation, one must first strengthen the body; to resist the enemy, one must strengthen national defense. In addition to material national defense, spiritual national defense relies on the flourishing of science and the daily progress of culture. May I ask, have our minds been rigorously trained? Intelligent young people should be able to infer the rest from these, without the need for further elaboration. Masters of the nation's future, please take good care of yourselves!"

3. Expectations for Other Publications: The prosperity of a nation relies on the collective efforts of the people, and individual success or failure is only a personal matter, but when a nation prospers or declines, no one can shirk their responsibility. Recalling the twenty-fourth year of the Republic of China, warlords ran rampant, and politicians caused chaos, leading to the downfall of the nation and the suffering of the people. Recently, imperialists have intensified their actions to infringe upon China, leading to the daily diminishing of our territory and the increasingly severe national crisis, which is beyond our ability to foresee. However, the people of our country are usually lazy to improve themselves, muddle-headed, and do not prepare for the unexpected, so that when things happen, they cannot be resolved. Following the Spring and Autumn Annals' tradition of criticizing the worthy, the people's guilt seems difficult to avoid being judged by future generations.

Now the New Year of the twenty-fifth year has quietly arrived amidst our heart-wrenching and tearful days. Looking ahead, we are even more pained! And our hopes for people from all walks of life are particularly earnest. We say: "Please, people from all walks of life, harbor a sense of danger like walking on thin ice, and starting from this New Year's Day of the twenty-fifth year of the Republic of China, make saving the country the only constant goal of your lives, and make firm resolutions. How should we revitalize industry and increase production to strengthen the nation? How should we educate the people and promote the principles of saving the country to awaken the people? How should we develop wasteland and connect waterways to benefit the masses? How should we...? All people from all walks of life should keep these 'how should we' questions in mind, go their separate ways, and fulfill their respective responsibilities. In the future, different paths will converge to form a strong foundation for saving the country. With this, what enemy cannot be destroyed? With this, what country cannot be saved? Oh, our loyal comrades from all walks of life, the time is critical, the situation is dangerous! If we do not catch up quickly, it will be too late!"

Overseas Correspondence Network

Black Slaves 226

— Changren

Correspondence from the Capital of Abyssinia

The most prevalent place for the slave trade in Africa is the Slave Coast. From the Niger River to Walvis Bay, its port of export is Luanda. The number of slaves transported from Luanda is truly numerous, like "carp crossing the river," but because the slave trade is a clandestine business, the exact numbers are impossible to count. The slaves exported from Luanda are mostly transported to Southern Europe, the central and northern parts of North America, and South America to work in mining and farming, living a subhuman life that is worse than that of cattle. The masters' treatment of the slaves consists only of providing basic sustenance, without any monetary compensation. Moreover, the sustenance provided is crude and insufficient, sometimes not even allowing them to eat their fill of the crudest foods. At night, to prevent them from escaping, the masters would rivet shackles on each person's feet, chaining dozens or several people together. Sometimes, when one person had to get up, everyone else would have to get up as well. This kind of restraint is stricter than that of a murderer. Therefore, among those who are sold into slavery, it is difficult for even one out of a thousand to survive.

There is a type of black people called Little Negro, an uncivilized tribe that still practices fetishism. Their national character is extremely fierce, but because they are as foolish as deer, they are easily deceived. Therefore, among the slaves that are transported and sold, nine out of ten belong to them. Even in the African mainland, they are often sold among themselves.

The Little Negroes in the Cameroon Mountains and the Adamawa Plateau live a life that has not departed from that of primitive humans. Each person's living tools consist of only a bow and arrow, and nothing else. With that sharp weapon, they can easily survive for decades. Every day, carrying a bow and arrow, they leap and dart like monkeys over mountains and ridges, searching for food. When they encounter wild animals or lone travelers, they treat them as objects of hunting and robbery. However, once they are transported and sold as slaves, they become as tame as sheep.

In addition, there are also many uncivilized tribes in northeastern Africa. They sell their children into slavery to do those heavy and strenuous jobs for others. When they reach seventeen or eighteen years old, they will be resold to distant places to reclaim wasteland, enduring drifting and wandering, and living a subhuman life. After being bought and enslaved, all his human rights belong to the master. If he accidentally offends the master, he may be flogged. Even if he is beaten to death by the master, the law will not have any sympathetic judgment. "Humanitarianism" is difficult to explain in slave circles. In some places, there is even a customary law that "killing a slave is not punishable by death and is not a crime."

The selling price of a little black slave is truly unbelievable. It is said that little black slaves aged nine to eleven are only worth about two silver dollars. Therefore, many whites who live in Africa love to buy such little black slaves to serve them.

Furthermore, along the Mediterranean, the Red Sea, and the East African coast, many black people are sold into slavery. They spend their whole days doing heavy and dangerous work for their masters until death or disability, without any compensation. There is also a type of young woman who is transported to various prosperous ports to satisfy the sexual desires of sailors and tea boys, and the price they get is unbelievably low. They are nicknamed Blackstone. After living such a life, when they reach a certain age, they sell a few little black female slaves to continue their lives of prostitution. In Suakin, Berber, and Port Sudan, as soon as the ship docks, you can easily see many barefoot, naked, and prostituting black female slaves with a red and green shawl draped over their shoulders.

Literary Works

Collecting Accounts (Conclusion) 228

— Puyü

The old man looked at me in alarm, then suddenly ran over frantically and pried open my hand, shouting in a voice like a broken gong: "I always knew what your 'official business' was!" The old man's throat was bulging, and he pounded his chest violently. "He's extorting money, he's oppressing the common people. Today official business, tomorrow official business, our calculations are all..."

Before he could finish, I slapped him in the face. The old man used all his strength to catch the slap, pushing me away so hard that I almost fell.

The old man was excessively exhausted, his face showing the color of death. His right hand trembled as he pointed at me, his voice weak and feeble: "You harmful people, I..." He dragged his stiff body towards me, but stumbled and fell to the ground.

Just as I was alarmed, several apprentices rushed in, supporting the old man while shouting: "You're driving people to their deaths! You're killing people! Beat him, beat that bastard!..."

Taking advantage of the chaos, I slipped out of the accounting room. By the time the second "Beat that..." reached my ears, I had already fled out the door! Just as I ran to the corner of the left wall, that kid Jiang Xiwu turned around and said: "Director, that was close!"

I wiped away a cold sweat and cursed heavily: "Damn bastard, only cares about himself!" (The End)

Broadcast Schedule

Editor's Note: Recently, I learned that a gentleman in the broadcasting world who shares the editor's surname and given name is involved in a love affair. This reminds me that some time ago, a reader wrote to inquire whether the editor was running a singing group. At the time, I thought it was hearsay and did not reply. It turns out that it was a real case. Now, I have seen my name widely publicized in certain broadcasting publications. I can assure you that I do not possess such "romantic" charm, and I hereby declare that it is not me.

Movie News

"Triumphant Song" Sweeps Across the Land 230

Since "Triumphant Song" premiered at the Golden City Theater, it has been praised not only for its realistic and tragic themes but also for its magnificent scenes and skillful techniques. Therefore, it is no wonder that it has received overwhelming praise, and it is widely regarded as the first great masterpiece in the history of Chinese films. As a result, the entrance of the Golden City Theater has been bustling with carriages and horses every day, and the popularity has been unprecedented. The fame of "Triumphant Song" has a sense of sweeping across the land. The picture on the left shows the lead actors Wang Yin and Qin Tong.

China Film Society for Renewal Holds Membership Recruitment Meeting 231

Since the China Film Society for Renewal first began recruiting male and female members, a large number of people have joined. Now, in order to further expand, it will hold a membership recruitment meeting starting today. It is divided into more than forty teams, with Chang Shaobai as the general captain, and the remaining teams are led by the members themselves. Those with excellent performance will be awarded prizes (the top three will be awarded silver shields). Anyone who loves film and drama, regardless of gender, can join. Because the original address is insufficient, it has been moved from the original address (Room 407, Taihe Building, Lloyd Road) to Room 204 on the second floor, still in Taihe Building on Lloyd Road. The new address has sufficient light and ample space. In the future, those who want to join or have matters to discuss can go to the new address listed above.

Silver Jottings 232

— Zhi'er

"Annual custom," it seems that one always has to write something about hope for the New Year, although these hopes can be typeset and printed annually, but one cannot be without hope.

For example, the Chinese film industry in 1935 passed through storms. 1936 may not see a turn for the better; however, hope is hope, that quality will improve month by month, and that output can increase.

As for whether it is implemented or not, that does not seem to have much to do with hope.

A certain newspaper, "Fragments," relayed: "But when all film companies are caught in the midst of 'no rice to cook,' it is a bit unrealistic to ask people to shoot new films."

The Chinese film industry in 1935 "a vigorous and stirring national salvation movement." After this article, I finally understood that there were brilliant people who knew the current affairs and were serving the times. My respects!

Really, the students who save the nation, why haven't they obediently returned to the classroom? Isn't the current situation in China all caught in the midst of "no rice to cook"? It is truly "extremely unrealistic"!
